## 🎯 THE PROBLEM (Realita Retail Trader)

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                       PAIN POINTS                                 ║
╠═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                   ║
║  1. TOO MANY TOOLS, NO INTEGRATION                                ║
║     Chart di TradingView → Sinyal di Telegram → Jurnal di Excel  ║
║     → Kalkulator risk di website lain → Berantakan.              ║
║                                                                   ║
║  2. INFORMASI OVERLOAD                                            ║
║     Setup 20+ indikator, 5 timeframe, 3 pair. Analisa paralys.   ║
║     Ujung-ujungnya: FOMO entry, revenge trading.                 ║
║                                                                   ║
║  3. GAK ADA MENTOR 24/7                                           ║
║     Mentor manusia: mahal, gak available tiap session.            ║
║     Free signal group: gak jelas, pump-and-dump.                 ║
║                                                                   ║
║  4. PSYCHOLOGY DIABAIKAN                                          ║
║     Semua fokus ke "entry mana?" — tapi gak ada yang nanya:      ║
║     "Lo lagi dalam kondisi mental apa hari ini?"                 ║
║                                                                   ║
║  5. CREDIBILITY ZERO                                              ║
║     "Lo profitable?" — trader gak bisa buktiin track record.     ║
║     Journal kosong, backtest gak ada, P&L gak ketahuan.          ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

# 🌳 OFFICIAL ECOSYSTEM TREE

```text
🐉 GOLDEN AI STRATEGY ECOSYSTEM
│
├── 👤 USER LAYER
│   ├── 🌐 Web App
│   ├── 📱 Mobile App
│   ├── 🤖 Telegram Bot
│   ├── 💬 WhatsApp AI
│   └── 🖥️ AI Terminal
│
├── 🛡️ GATEWAY & AUTH LAYER
│
├── ⚙️ APPLICATION LAYER
│   ├── 💬 Chat Workspace
│   ├── 📊 Trading Dashboard
│   ├── 🎯 Signal Center
│   ├── 📓 Journal System
│   ├── 📈 Analytics Center
│   └── 🎓 Education Hub
│
├── 🧠 AI ORCHESTRATION LAYER
│   ├── 🔀 AI Router
│   ├── 🤖 AI Agents
│   ├── 📝 Prompt Engine
│   ├── 🧩 Context Engine
│   └── 🧠 Memory Engine
│
├── 📡 DATA & EXECUTION LAYER
│   ├── 🔗 MT5 Bridge
│   ├── 📊 Market Data Engine
│   ├── 🌍 Macro Engine
│   ├── 🎯 Signal Engine
│   ├── 🔔 Notification Engine
│   └── ⚠️ Risk Engine
│
└── 🗄️ INFRASTRUCTURE LAYER
    ├── 🐘 PostgreSQL
    ├── ⚡ Redis
    ├── 🔌 WebSocket
    ├── 🐳 Docker
    ├── ☁️ VPS/Cloud
    └── 📊 Monitoring
```

## 1. 💬 CHAT WORKSPACE

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   "Your AI Trading Co-Pilot, Always Online"                      ║
║                                                                   ║
║   The central interface. Chat dengan AI yang ngerti trading.      ║
║   Bukan chatbot biasa — ini AI yang bisa baca chart, deteksi     ║
║   SMC structure, dan kasih trading plan lengkap.                 ║
║                                                                   ║
╠═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                   ║
║   CORE FEATURES                                                   ║
║   ─────────────                                                   ║
║   • Natural language chat (ID/EN bilingual)                      ║
║   • Vision AI — upload chart screenshot → instant analysis       ║
║   • Auto-screenshot TradingView chart via command                ║
║   • Multi-turn conversation with context memory                  ║
║   • SSE streaming (real-time token-by-token response)            ║
║   • Code & syntax highlighting (Pine Script, Python, MQL)        ║
║   • Voice input (mobile)                                          ║
║   • Image generation (chart markup, trade ideas)                 ║
║                                                                   ║
║   AI CAPABILITIES                                                 ║
║   ──────────────                                                  ║
║   • "Analisa XAUUSD H4 intraday" → full pipeline                 ║
║   • "Kenapa price turun padahal NFP bagus?" → explain            ║
║   • "Backtest strategy gua 3 bulan terakhir" → run backtest     ║
║   • "Cek psikologi gua minggu ini" → psychology report           ║
║   • "Ajarin gua tentang ICT Silver Bullet" → education           ║
║   • "Bikinin kode Pine Script untuk setup ini" → code gen       ║
║                                                                   ║
║   FOR WHO: All users. Entry point ke seluruh ekosistem.           ║
║   PLAN: Essential (basic) → Ultimate (full vision + memory)      ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 3. 🎯 SIGNAL CENTER

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   "Structured Trade Ideas, Not Blind Calls"                      ║
║                                                                   ║
║   Signal yang dikasih bukan cuma "BUY NOW". Tiap signal          ║
║   dilengkapi: observation, reasoning, trading plan, risk          ║
║   calculation, dan confidence grade.                              ║
║                                                                   ║
╠═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                   ║
║   CORE FEATURES                                                   ║
║   ─────────────                                                   ║
║   • Signal feed (real-time, sorted by confidence)                ║
║   • AI-generated signals (on-demand + scheduled)                 ║
║   • Pine Script webhook signals (TradingView → GAS)              ║
║   • Confluence scoring (SMC + Indicators + Pattern + Regime)     ║
║   • Multi-timeframe confirmation visual                          ║
║   • A+ / A / B grading system                                    ║
║   • Signal history with win rate tracking                        ║
║   • Custom alert rules (pair, grade, session)                    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   SIGNAL CARD CONTENTS                                            ║
║   ─────────────────────                                            ║
║   • Direction (BUY/SELL) + Bias (Bullish/Bearish)                ║
║   • Entry zone (price range)                                      ║
║   • Stop Loss (price + pips)                                      ║
║   • TP1 / TP2 / TP3 (price + pips)                               ║
║   • Risk:Reward ratio                                             ║
║   • Lot size suggestion (per $1K balance)                        ║
║   • Confidence % + Grade                                          ║
║   • Key confluences (why this trade)                              ║
║   • Invalidation point                                            ║
║   • Time validity (e.g. "Valid for 24h")                         ║
║                                                                   ║
║   FOR WHO: Traders who want structured, verified trade ideas.     ║
║   PLAN: Essential (basic) → Ultimate (A+ grade, Pine+AI)         ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 4. 📓 JOURNAL SYSTEM

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   "Your Trading Ledger — Automatic & Insightful"                 ║
║                                                                   ║
║   Journaling itu hal paling penting tapi paling malesin.         ║
║   GAS auto-capture trade lo dari MT5, jadi gak perlu manual.     ║
║   AI analisa pola trading lo dan kasih improvement plan.         ║
║                                                                   ║
╠═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                   ║
║   CORE FEATURES                                                   ║
║   ─────────────                                                   ║
║   • Auto-capture dari MT5 (entry, exit, P&L, duration)           ║
║   • Manual entry via chat ("/journal XAUUSD buy +50 pips")      ║
║   • Screenshot attachment (chart at entry + exit)                ║
║   • Emotion tagging (FOMO, Calm, Revenge, Confident, etc)       ║
║   • Setup tagging (SMC, ICT, Support/Resistance, etc)            ║
║   • Mistake tagging (No SL, Oversize, Early exit, etc)           ║
║   • AI summary per session / per week                            ║
║   • Pattern detection (AI spots recurring mistakes)              ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ANALYTICS FROM JOURNAL                                           ║
║   ────────────────────────                                         ║
║   • Win rate by pair, session, day, setup type                   ║
║   • Average R:R realized vs planned                               ║
║   • Biggest mistake pattern                                       ║
║   • Best performing setup                                         ║
║   • Emotion vs P&L correlation                                    ║
║   • Weekly improvement score                                      ║
║                                                                   ║
║   FOR WHO: Traders serious about growth and accountability.       ║
║   PLAN: Premium+ (auto-capture + AI analysis)                     ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

# 1️⃣ GOLDEN AI MARKET PULSE

> **"AI Market Intelligence Dashboard"**
> See the market. Understand it. Plan your move. Measure your edge.
> Dashboard + Chat Workspace + Analytics Center

## 🎯 Purpose

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   Menjawab 3 pertanyaan fundamental setiap trader:                ║
║                                                                   ║
║   1. "APA yang terjadi di market sekarang?"                      ║
║      → Live Dashboard: harga, sesi, kalender, sentimen           ║
║                                                                   ║
║   2. "KENAPA ini terjadi dan apa yang harus gw lakuin?"          ║
║      → AI Chat: observasi, reasoning, trading plan               ║
║                                                                   ║

║      → Analytics: P&L, win rate, psychology, improvement         ║
║                                                                   ║

║   Dari "gak tau harus ngapain" → "gw tau persis setup gw."      ║

## 🔄 Workflow

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   GOLDEN AI MARKET PULSE — DAILY TRADER FLOW                     ║
║                                                                   ║

║   │                                                           │  ║

║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                            │                                      ║
║                            ▼                                      ║
║   📋 3. TRADING PLAN GENERATED (AI)                               ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  AI returns structured plan:                               │  ║
║   │                                                           │  ║

║   │  📋 TRADING PLAN    → Entry, SL, TP1, TP2, TP3, RR       │  ║
║   │  ⚠️ RISK            → Lot size, max loss, rules check     │  ║
║   │  📓 JOURNAL PREVIEW → Expected outcome + setup grade     │  ║
║   │                                                           │  ║
║   │  Decision Support:                                         │  ║
║   │  🟢 GO     — All checks passed, within risk limits       │  ║
║   │  🟡 CAUTION — Minor concern (spread, news proximity)     │  ║
║   │  🔴 NO-GO  — Setup violates rules / risk limits          │  ║
║   │                                                           │  ║
║   │  Trader reviews plan → sets pending order on broker      │  ║
║   │  ⏱️ 2-5 min                                              │  ║
║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                            │                                      ║
║                            ▼                                      ║
║   📓 4. EXECUTION & JOURNAL (Trade Active)                        ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  MT5 auto-sync → Market Pulse detects trade opened        │  ║
║   │                                                           │  ║
║   │  Live tracking:                                            │  ║

║   │                                                           │  ║

║                            │                                      ║

```

║   ─────────────────────────                                       ║

# 2️⃣ GOLDEN AI INDICATOR ENGINE

> **"The Technical Brain — Compute, detect, feed every signal."**
> Technical Indicators · SMC/ICT · Pattern Detection · Regime Analysis

## 🎯 Purpose

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   The computation core. Raw price → structured intelligence.      ║
║                                                                   ║
║   1. Compute 50+ indicators real-time (ADX, RSI, MACD, BB...)    ║
║   2. Detect SMC/ICT structures (OB, FVG, Liq, Breaker)          ║
║   3. Identify chart patterns (H&S, Wedge, Double Top, Flag)     ║
║   4. Classify market regime (Trending/Ranging/Volatile)          ║
║   5. Feed structured data → AI Pipeline + Market Pulse           ║
║                                                                   ║
║   All engines run async parallel · Result in < 10 seconds.       ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## ⚡ Features

### 🏗️ Structure Detection

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   Auto-detect & label the full market structure narrative.        ║
║                                                                   ║
║   TREND STRUCTURE                                                  ║
║   ──────────────                                                   ║
║   • HH / HL → Bullish structure (uptrend)                        ║
║   • LH / LL → Bearish structure (downtrend)                      ║
║   • BOS (Break of Structure) → Trend continuation confirmed      ║
║   • CHOCH (Change of Character) → Potential reversal signal      ║
║   • IDM (Inducement) → Liquidity trap before real move           ║
║                                                                   ║
║   SMC/ICT CONCEPTS                                                ║
║   ────────────────                                                 ║
║   • Order Blocks (OB) — Last candle before impulse move          ║
║   • Fair Value Gaps (FVG) — Unfilled inefficiency zones          ║
║   • Liquidity Sweeps — Stop hunt above EQH / below EQL          ║
║   • Breaker Blocks — Failed OB that flips role                   ║
║   • Mitigation Blocks — OB that has been tested & held           ║
║   • Equilibrium — 50% of dealing range (rebalancing target)     ║
║   • Rejection Blocks — Price strongly rejected this zone         ║
║                                                                   ║
║   OUTPUT PER TIMEFRAME:                                           ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │  D1:  🟢 BULLISH   HH↑ HL↑   OB: 2620-2625              │   ║
║   │  H4:  🟢 BULLISH   BOS 2650  FVG: 2640-2645             │   ║
║   │  H1:  🟡 PULLBACK  CHOCH?    Testing H4 OB at 2645      │   ║
║   │  M15: ⚪ WAIT      —         Wait for M5 confirmation     │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ENGINE: SMC Engine :8006 · Pattern Detector :9501              ║
║   INPUT:  OHLC data (MT5 :8100)                                   ║
║   OUTPUT: JSON structure → AI Pipeline + Market Pulse overlay     ║
║   ⏱️ :  < 3 seconds                                              ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

### ⭐ Market Analyst Agent

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   MARKET ANALYST AGENT — The most-used agent in the ecosystem    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   Division:  WIN 3 (Trading)                                     ║
║   Priority:  CRITICAL — powers all analysis requests             ║
║                                                                   ║
╠═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                   ║
║   ROLE                                                             ║
║   ────                                                             ║
║   "I am the Chief Market Analyst. I combine technicals,          ║
║    fundamentals, sentiment, and structure into one clear,         ║
║    actionable analysis. I don't guess. I synthesize data."        ║
║                                                                   ║
║   TASKS                                                            ║
║   ─────                                                            ║
║   • Full multi-TF analysis (4 timeframes)                        ║
║   • SMC/ICT structure breakdown                                  ║
║   • Indicator computation + interpretation                      ║
║   • Pattern detection + validation                               ║
║   • Macro context integration                                    ║
║   • Bias generation with confidence scoring                      ║
║   • Trading plan formulation (Entry, SL, TP, RR)                 ║
║   • Risk validation against user rules                           ║
║   • Session-aware recommendations                                 ║
║                                                                   ║
║   TOOLS                                                            ║
║   ─────                                                            ║
║   fetch_chart · fetch_mt5_data · call_smc_engine                  ║
║   call_indicator · call_pattern · call_regime                     ║
║   call_calendar · call_fundamental · call_sentiment               ║
║   call_correlation · call_risk · send_alert                       ║
║   search_rag_macro · search_rag_technical · cache_get/set         ║
║                                                                   ║
║   WORKFLOW                                                         ║
║   ────────                                                         ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │  TRIGGER: User requests analysis or alert fires          │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  STEP 1: Gather Context (parallel)                       │   ║
║   │  ├── fetch_mt5_data → live OHLC + tick                   │   ║
║   │  ├── call_calendar → upcoming news events                │   ║
║   │  ├── call_sentiment → market mood                         │   ║
║   │  └── cache_get → check for recent analysis               │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  STEP 2: Technical Layer (parallel)                      │   ║
║   │  ├── call_smc_engine → OB, FVG, Liq, Structure           │   ║
║   │  ├── call_indicator → 50+ indicator readings             │   ║
║   │  ├── call_pattern → chart + candle patterns              │   ║
║   │  ├── call_regime → market phase classification           │   ║
║   │  └── call_correlation → DXY, VIX, bonds                  │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  STEP 3: Macro Layer (parallel)                          │   ║
║   │  ├── call_fundamental → CPI, GDP, COT, rates             │   ║
║   │  ├── search_rag_macro → historical context               │   ║
║   │  └── search_rag_technical → similar setups               │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  STEP 4: AI Synthesis (Claude Sonnet 4.6)                │   ║
║   │  ├── Feed all data + style-specific prompt               │   ║
║   │  ├── Generate: observation, reasoning, trading plan      │   ║
║   │  └── Validate: RR, risk rules, session fit               │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  STEP 5: Output                                          │   ║
║   │  ├── Format JSON → Markdown/HTML                         │   ║
║   │  ├── Stream to user → Market Pulse Chat                  │   ║
║   │  ├── Save to PostgreSQL → analyses table                 │   ║
║   │  ├── Cache to Redis → TTL 60s                            │   ║
║   │  └── call_risk → final risk validation                   │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   MODEL:   Claude Sonnet 4.6 (primary) · GPT-4o-mini (fast)     ║
║   INPUT:   pair + timeframe + style + market_data                  ║
║   OUTPUT:  { observation, reasoning, trading_plan, risk }         ║
║   ⏱️ :     40-70 seconds (Vision AI adds +20-30s)                ║
║   COST:    $0.09 (Claude) / $0.02 (GPT-4o-mini)                  ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

### 🧭 Bias Engine Agent

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   BIAS ENGINE AGENT — The "No More Guesswork" Agent              ║
║                                                                   ║

║   Priority:  HIGH — generates directional call for EVERY analysis║
║                                                                   ║
╠═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣

║   ────                                                             ║

║    layer of analysis and produce ONE clear direction with         ║

║                                                                   ║
║   TASKS                                                            ║
║   ─────                                                            ║
║   • Score 4 layers: Structure + Indicators + Patterns + Context  ║
║   • Weight each signal by reliability (learned from journal)     ║

║   • Detect divergence between layers (e.g. bullish TA, bearish  ║
║     macro → flag as CAUTIOUS)                                     ║
║   • Generate final bias: BULLISH / CAUTIOUS / NEUTRAL / BEARISH ║
║   • Produce confidence % with explanation                        ║
║                                                                   ║
║   SCORING METHODOLOGY                                              ║
║   ───────────────────                                              ║

║   │                                                          │   ║

║   │  ───────────────────────────                              │   ║

║   │                                                          │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗

║    where stops are being hunted, and where price is likely to    ║
║    go next. I don't predict. I interpret structure."             ║
║                                                                   ║
║   WHAT IT DETECTS                                                  ║
║   ───────────────                                                  ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  TREND STRUCTURE                                         │   ║
║   │  ──────────────                                          │   ║
║   │  HH (Higher High)    → Bullish continuation              │   ║
║   │  HL (Higher Low)     → Bullish pullback healthy           │   ║
║   │  LH (Lower High)     → Bearish continuation              │   ║
║   │  LL (Lower Low)      → Bearish continuation              │   ║
║   │  BOS (Break)         → Trend confirmed, next leg         │   ║
║   │  CHOCH (Change)      → Potential reversal signal         │   ║
║   │  IDM (Inducement)    → Fake move before real direction   │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  SMC CONCEPTS                                            │   ║
║   │  ────────────                                            │   ║
║   │  Order Block (OB)    → Institutional entry zone          │   ║
║   │  Fair Value Gap (FVG)→ Unfilled inefficiency = magnet    │   ║
║   │  Breaker Block       → Failed OB, now support/resistance │   ║
║   │  Mitigation Block    → OB tested & held → stronger       │   ║
║   │  Rejection Block     → Strong rejection → reversal zone  │   ║
║   │  Equilibrium         → 50% of dealing range              │   ║
║   │  Discount/Premium    → Price relative to dealing range   │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  LIQUIDITY MAPPING                                       │   ║
║   │  ────────────────                                        │   ║
║   │  Equal Highs (EQH)   → Buy-side liquidity pool           │   ║
║   │  Equal Lows (EQL)    → Sell-side liquidity pool           │   ║
║   │  Session High/Low    → Asian/London/NY range extremes     │   ║
║   │  Previous Day H/L    → Yesterday's stop-hunt zones       │   ║
║   │  Trendline Liq       → Stops behind swing points         │   ║
║   │  Double Top/Bottom   → Classic liquidity traps           │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  KILL ZONES                                              │   ║
║   │  ──────────                                              │   ║
║   │  London KZ (07-10 GMT)    → Best reversal setups         │   ║
║   │  NY KZ (12-15 GMT)        → Strong continuation          │   ║
║   │  Asian Range (00-07 GMT)  → Accumulation zone            │   ║
║   │  LON+NY Overlap           → Highest probability window   │   ║
║   │  Silver Bullet (10-11,    → ICT 1H reversal pattern      │   ║
║   │    13-14, 19-20 GMT)                                      │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   STRUCTURE SNAPSHOT OUTPUT:                                       ║
║   ─────────────────────────                                       ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║

║   │       HH at 2680, HL at 2620. OB: 2620-2625.             │   ║

║   │                                                          │   ║

# 2️⃣ GOLDEN AI SIGNAL ENGINE

> **"Generate Institutional-Style Signal Intelligence."**
> Not a signal group. Not copy-trade. Structured, validated, tracked.
> Signal Generation · Validation · Distribution · Tracking

## 🎯 Purpose

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗

### 🏅 Signal Grading System

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   Every signal gets a GRADE. Not all setups are equal.            ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌────────┬──────────┬──────────┬──────────┬─────────────────┐  ║
║   │ GRADE  │ CONF.    │ CONFLU.  │ ACTION   │ MEANING          │  ║
║   ├────────┼──────────┼──────────┼──────────┼─────────────────┤  ║
║   │ A+ 🟢  │ 80-100%  │ 4/4 TF   │ LIVE     │ "Perfect setup.  │  ║
║   │        │          │ aligned  │ SIGNAL   │  Trade full size."│  ║
║   ├────────┼──────────┼──────────┼──────────┼─────────────────┤  ║
║   │ A  🟢  │ 70-79%   │ 3/4 TF   │ LIVE     │ "Strong setup.    │  ║
║   │        │          │ aligned  │ SIGNAL   │  Standard trade." │  ║
║   ├────────┼──────────┼──────────┼──────────┼─────────────────┤  ║
║   │ B  🟡  │ 55-69%   │ 2/4 TF   │ WAIT     │ "Decent setup.    │  ║
║   │        │          │ mixed    │ CARD     │  Wait for trigger"│  ║
║   ├────────┼──────────┼──────────┼──────────┼─────────────────┤  ║
║   │ C  🔴  │ <55%     │ Weak     │ FILTER   │ "Not enough.      │  ║
║   │        │          │ signals  │ OUT      │  Don't distract." │  ║
║   ├────────┼──────────┼──────────┼──────────┼─────────────────┤  ║
║   │ REJECT │ —        │ Conflict │ SILENT   │ "Contradiction.   │  ║
║   │        │          │ detected │ DROP     │  Protect trader." │  ║
║   └────────┴──────────┴──────────┴──────────┴─────────────────┘  ║
║                                                                   ║
║   GRADING INPUTS:                                                  ║
║   ──────────────                                                   ║
║   • Bias Engine score (4-layer weighted)                          ║
║   • Multi-TF confirmation (how many TFs agree)                   ║
║   • AI Vision validation (Claude reviews chart screenshots)      ║
║   • Pine Script grade (if from TradingView webhook)              ║
║   • Risk check (RR meets minimum? DD within limit?)              ║
║   • News proximity (high impact ±30m → downgrade)                ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 1.1 📊 TRADING DASHBOARD

## 🔄 Workflow

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   SIGNAL LIFECYCLE — Generate → Validate → Distribute → Track    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   0. MARKET CONDITIONS   Assess regime + volatility + news      ║
║   1. PATTERN DETECTION   Chart patterns + candlestick + harmonic║
║   2. GENERATE            AI + Pine Script → full signal card    ║
║   3. SIGNAL VALIDATION   AI reviews + confirms signal quality   ║
║   4. GRADE               A+/A/B/C/REJECT grading               ║
║   5. RISK VALIDATION     Lot size · RR · DD · Rules check       ║
║   6. AI CONFIDENCE       Signal + Risk + Trader Fit = Score    ║
║   7. SIGNAL DELIVERY     Web · TG · Push · WA · Email           ║
║   8. TRADER ACTS         Execute / Dismiss / Snooze             ║
║   9. CAPTURE             MT5 auto-sync → journal → track P&L   ║
║   10. LEARN              Outcome → adjust grading + bias        ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔁 Continuous loop: Generate → Act → Learn → Improve → Repeat  ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🤖 AI Agents Used

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   SIGNAL ENGINE — AGENT ORCHESTRATION                            ║
║                                                                   ║
║   Every signal passes through multiple specialized AI agents.     ║
║                                                                   ║
╠═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                   ║
║   ⭐ MARKET ANALYST AGENT                                          ║
║   ───────────────────────                                          ║
║   Step:  2 (Generate) · 3 (Validation)                           ║
║   Role:  Runs full analysis pipeline, generates signal card      ║
║   Output: { observation, reasoning, trading_plan, risk }         ║
║   Model:  Claude Sonnet 4.6 · ⏱️ 40-70s · 💰 $0.09              ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🎯 SIGNAL AGENT                                                  ║
║   ──────────────                                                  ║
║   Step:  3 (Validation) · 4 (Grade) · 6 (Confidence)            ║
║   Role:  Generates + grades + validates signal quality           ║
║   Output: { signal_card, grade, confidence, risk_score }        ║
║   Model:  GPT-4o-mini (fast) / Claude Sonnet (deep)             ║
║   ⏱️ :    3-5 seconds · 💰 $0.003                               ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ✅ VALIDATION AGENT                                              ║
║   ─────────────────                                                ║
║   Step:  3 (Signal Validation)                                    ║
║   Role:  Cross-check signal across all analysis layers           ║
║          Verify consistency · Detect contradictions ·            ║
║          Flag overfitting · Validate RR against style rules      ║
║   Output: { is_valid, warnings, confidence_adjustment }         ║
║   Model:  Claude Haiku 4.5 · ⏱️ <2s · 💰 $0.004                ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔍 CONFIRMATION AGENT                                            ║
║   ────────────────────                                             ║
║   Step:  6 (AI Confidence)                                        ║
║   Role:  Wait + verify second-layer confirmations before GO      ║
║          Multi-TF alignment check · Entry trigger monitor ·       ║
║          Divergence scan · Fakeout detection · Re-test verify    ║
║   Output: { confirmed, trigger_status, wait_time, expiry }       ║
║   Model:  GPT-4o-mini · ⏱️ 2-5s (monitors real-time) · 💰 $0.002║
║                                                                   ║
║   🧭 BIAS ENGINE AGENT                                            ║
║   ───────────────────                                             ║
║   Step:  0 (Market Conditions) · 4 (Grade)                       ║
║   Role:  Scores 4 layers, generates directional bias             ║
║   Output: { bias, confidence, grade, layer_scores }              ║
║   Model:  Claude Haiku 4.5 · ⏱️ <2s · 💰 $0.004                 ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🏗️ STRUCTURE DETECTION AGENT                                    ║
║   ───────────────────────────                                     ║
║   Step:  1 (Pattern Detection)                                    ║
║   Role:  Reads market structure narrative, detects SMC patterns  ║
║   Output: { structure_state, OB, FVG, liq_zones }                ║
║   Model:  Claude Haiku 4.5 · ⏱️ <3s · 💰 $0.005                 ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📊 VOLATILITY AGENT                                              ║
║   ─────────────────                                               ║
║   Step:  0 (Market Conditions) · 5 (Risk Validation)             ║
║   Role:  Measures market temperature, adjusts risk params        ║
║   Output: { volatility_regime, auto_adjustments }               ║
║   Model:  Pure code · ⏱️ <1s · 💰 $0.000                        ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🛡️ RISK AGENT                                                   ║
║   ────────────                                                    ║
║   Step:  5 (Risk Validation) · 6 (AI Confidence)                 ║
║   Role:  Validates risk rules, generates risk score              ║
║   Output: { risk_score, lot_size, go_no_go }                     ║
║   Model:  Pure code · ⏱️ <1s · 💰 $0.000                        ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📡 NOTIFY AGENT                                                  ║
║   ──────────────                                                  ║
║   Step:  7 (Signal Delivery)                                      ║
║   Role:  Routes signals to all user channels with filters        ║
║   Output: Delivered/Queued/Failed per channel                    ║
║   Model:  Pure code · ⏱️ <0.5s · 💰 $0.000                      ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🧠 STRATEGY AGENT                                                ║
║   ────────────────                                                ║
║   Step:  10 (Learn)                                               ║
║   Role:  Analyzes signal outcomes, tunes grading algorithm       ║
║   Output: { adjusted_weights, improved_metrics }                 ║
║   Model:  GPT-4o-mini · ⏱️ ~5s · 💰 $0.002 (batch/weekly)      ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────  ║
║                                                                   ║
║   TOTAL AI COST PER SIGNAL:                                       ║
║   ────────────────────────                                        ║
║   Claude Sonnet 4.6  (analyst)  = $0.090                         ║
║   Claude Haiku 4.5   (bias)     = $0.004                         ║
║   Claude Haiku 4.5   (structure)= $0.005                         ║
║   Pure code           (rest)     = $0.000                         ║
║   ─────────────────────────────────────────                       ║
║   TOTAL PER SIGNAL               = $0.099                        ║
║                                                                   ║
║   With caching (TTL 60s for same pair+TF): ~$0.050/signal        ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

║   │  ─────────────────────────────────────                   │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  📖 WHAT IS IT?                                          │   ║
║   │  Silver Bullet = ICT reversal setup during kill zones.   │   ║
║   │  Entry at fair value gap after liquidity sweep.          │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  ⏰ WHEN TO TRADE                                         │   ║
║   │  London KZ: 08:00-11:00 GMT · NY KZ: 13:00-16:00 GMT    │   ║
║   │  Best: First 2 hours of London kill zone                 │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  🔍 ENTRY RULES                                          │   ║
║   │  1. Wait for liquidity sweep above/below KZ range        │   ║
║   │  2. Look for displacement (strong candle)                │   ║
║   │  3. Enter at FVG retest                                   │   ║
║   │  4. SL: Beyond the sweep level                            │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  📊 RISK PARAMETERS                                      │   ║
║   │  • Max risk: 1-2% per trade                              │   ║
║   │  • Target RR: 1:2 minimum                                │   ║
║   │  • Best TF: H1 or M15                                     │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  📈 REAL EXAMPLE (Today)                                  │   ║
║   │  XAUUSD swept Asian low, displaced down,                  │   ║
║   │  retraced to 15-min FVG. Entry: 2645.50.                 │   ║
║   │  SL: 2640. TP1: 2655. TP2: 2665. RR: 1:2.1 ✅            │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  ❌ COMMON MISTAKES                                       │   ║
║   │  • Entering before FVG retest (chasing)                  │   ║
║   │  • Trading outside kill zones (lower probability)        │   ║
║   │  • TP too close (leave runners for bigger moves)         │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   SETUPS COVERED:                                                  ║
║   ──────────────                                                   ║
║   ICT Silver Bullet · OB+Breaker · S/R Flip · Trend Continuation  ║
║   Double Top/Bottom · Head & Shoulders · Wedge Break · Flag       ║
║                                                                   ║

║                                                                   ║

## 🔄 Workflow

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   TRADING ASSISTANT — THE TRADER GROWTH PATH                     ║
║                                                                   ║
║   👤 0. USER QUESTION                                              ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  "Gimana cara entry pake OB?"                              │  ║
║   │  "Backtest strategi gua 3 bulan terakhir"                  │  ║
║   │  "Kenapa gua masih rugi terus?"                            │  ║

║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                            │                                      ║
║                            ▼                                      ║
║   📚 0.5 KNOWLEDGE RETRIEVAL                                      ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  RAG Pipeline: search vector DB for relevant context      │  ║
║   │  • ICT/SMC knowledge base                                  │  ║
║   │  • Trading textbooks + course material                     │  ║
║   │  • User's journal history (personalized context)           │  ║
║   │  • Market context (current regime, news, volatility)      │  ║
║   │                                                           │  ║
║   │  ⏱️ < 1 second (Redis cached embeddings)                   │  ║
║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                            │                                      ║
║                            ▼                                      ║
║   📈 0.6 CHART CONTEXT                                             ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  Auto-load relevant chart data for the question           │  ║
║   │  • Current pair chart (if applicable)                     │  ║
║   │  • Multi-TF view (style-dependent)                        │  ║
║   │  • Key levels marked (S/R, OB, FVG)                       │  ║
║   │  • Structure + bias snapshot                               │  ║
║   │                                                           │  ║
║   │  ⏱️ < 3 seconds (MT5 data + indicator compute)             │  ║
║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                            │                                      ║
║                            ▼                                      ║
║   🧠 0.7 AI REASONING                                              ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║

║   │  • User question + intent                                  │  ║
║   │  • Retrieved knowledge (RAG)                               │  ║
║   │  • Chart context (live market data)                        │  ║
║   │  • User profile (experience, style, history)              │  ║
║   │                                                           │  ║
║   │  Deep reasoning → Structured, actionable answer           │  ║
║   │  ⏱️ 5-15 seconds                                          │  ║
║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                            │                                      ║

║   │                                                           │  ║

║   │  → Monthly edge validation · Regime shift alerts          │  ║
║   │                                                           │  ║
║   │  Prop Firm Readiness: Are you ready to apply?             │  ║
║   │  → Track vs FTMO/FundedNext criteria                      │  ║
║   │  → "2 more clean weeks and you're ready."                 │  ║
║   │                                                           │  ║
║   │  ⏱️ Weekly review · Monthly deep dive                       │  ║
║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔁 Ask → Retrieve → Learn → Test → Track → Analyze → Grow    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   This is how you become a consistently profitable trader.        ║
║   Not by luck. By system. By accountability. By growth.           ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

# 5️⃣ GOLDEN STRATEGY DASHBOARD

> **"Trader Operating Dashboard. Your Trading Command Center."**
> Live Market Watch · Positions · Calendar · Performance · Multi-Asset

## 🎯 Purpose

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   The Strategy Dashboard is your home screen for trading.         ║
║                                                                   ║
║   Menjawab 4 pertanyaan setiap trader saat buka platform:         ║
║                                                                   ║
║   1. "MARKET SEKARANG GIMANA?"                                    ║
║      → Live prices, charts, sessions, news, correlation          ║
║                                                                   ║
║   2. "POSISI GUA GIMANA?"                                         ║
║      → Active positions, live P&L, risk exposure, DD tracker     ║
║                                                                   ║
║   3. "ADA EVENT PENTING HARI INI?"                                ║
║      → Economic calendar, impact rating, countdown timer         ║
║                                                                   ║
║   4. "PERFORMANCE GUA GIMANA?"                                    ║
║      → Win rate, equity curve, P&L breakdown, metrics at glance  ║
║                                                                   ║

║                                                                   ║
║   One dashboard. All your trading intelligence. Zero clutter.     ║
║                                                                   ║

```

## 🔄 Workflow

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   STRATEGY DASHBOARD — TRADER DAILY OS                            ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📡 0. TRADE DATA (Continuous)                                    ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  MT5 Bridge streams real-time data → Dashboard:           │  ║
║   │  • Tick data → live prices (Redis Streams)                │  ║
║   │  • OHLC → charts + historical                              │  ║
║   │  • Positions → active trades + P&L                         │  ║
║   │  • Orders → pending orders + modifications                │  ║
║   │  • Account → balance, equity, margin                      │  ║
║   │                                                           │  ║
║   │  ⏱️ Real-time · < 50ms latency                             │  ║
║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                            │                                      ║
║                            ▼                                      ║
║   📓 0.5 JOURNAL ENGINE (Auto-Capture)                              ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  When trade opens/closes → Journal auto-records:           │  ║
║   │  • Entry time, price, direction, lot, setup tag           │  ║
║   │  • Exit time, price, P&L, duration                        │  ║
║   │  • Auto-attach chart screenshots (entry + exit)           │  ║
║   │  • Prompt emotion tag + trade notes                        │  ║
║   │                                                           │  ║
║   │  ⏱️ Auto · Zero manual entry                               │  ║
║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                            │                                      ║
║                            ▼                                      ║
║   📈 0.6 ANALYTICS ENGINE (Continuous)                              ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  Processes trade data → live metrics:                     │  ║
║   │  • Win rate, profit factor, Sharpe, drawdown              │  ║
║   │  • Equity curve update                                     │  ║
║   │  • Goal tracker progress                                   │  ║

║   │ TASK TYPE          │ PRIMARY MODEL      │ FALLBACK          │ ║

║   │ Fast/Quick Tasks   │ GPT-4o-mini        │ Claude Haiku     │ ║
║   │ Strategy/Backtest  │ Gemini 2.5 Pro     │ Claude Sonnet    │ ║

║   │ Journal AI         │ Claude Haiku 4.5   │ GPT-4o-mini      │ ║
║   │ Code Gen (PS/MQL)  │ GPT-4o-mini        │ Claude Haiku     │ ║
║   │ Embedding/RAG      │ text-embed-3-small │ (OpenAI only)    │ ║
║   │ Pure Computation   │ NO AI              │ (free)           │ ║

║                                                                   ║
║   CIRCUIT BREAKER: 5 failures → 300s timeout → fallback model    ║
║   RESPONSE CACHE: Redis TTL 60s (identical pair+TF+style)       ║
║   CREDIT TIER: Budget→DeepSeek · Standard→Haiku/GPT · Pro→Sonnet║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🔄 EVENT BUS — Agent Communication

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   Redis Streams — Pub/Sub for all agent communication            ║
║                                                                   ║
║   EVENT FLOW EXAMPLE:                                              ║
║   ──────────────────                                               ║
║   User: "/analyze XAUUSD H4 intraday"                             ║
║        │                                                          ║
║        ▼                                                          ║
║   EventBus.publish("analysis_requested", {pair, tf, style})       ║
║        │                                                          ║
║        ├──► Market Analyst Agent subscribes → starts analysis     ║
║        ├──► Bias Engine Agent subscribes → starts scoring         ║
║        ├──► Structure Agent subscribes → starts detection         ║
║        ├──► Volatility Agent subscribes → starts measuring        ║
║        └──► Risk Agent subscribes → starts validating             ║
║             │                                                      ║
║             ▼                                                      ║
║   All agents publish results → EventBus aggregates → Response     ║
║                                                                   ║
║   KEY FEATURES:                                                    ║
║   ────────────                                                     ║
║   • At-least-once delivery (consumer groups)                      ║
║   • Automatic load balancing (multiple instances)                 ║
║   • Pending message tracking (no lost tasks)                      ║
║   • Event replay capability (debug/reprocess)                      ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🔄 Orchestration Flow

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   USER REQUEST → RESPONSE LIFECYCLE                              ║
║                                                                   ║
║   0. USER REQUEST                                                  ║
║   ──────────────                                                   ║
║   "/analyze XAUUSD H4 intraday"                                   ║
║   "Backtest strategi gua 3 bulan"                                  ║
║   "Kenapa gua masih rugi terus?"                                   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   1. REQUEST ARRIVES                                               ║
║   ────────────────                                                 ║
║   Gateway :8000 → Auth + Credit check → Route to Agent Engine    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   2. INTENT DETECTION                                              ║
║   ─────────────────                                                ║
║   GPT-4o-mini parses user message → determines exact intent       ║
║   Model: GPT-4o-mini · ⏱️ <1s · 💰 $0.001                        ║
║                                                                   ║
║   3. TASK CLASSIFICATION                                           ║
║   ─────────────────────                                            ║
║   Intent mapped → Task categorized: complexity + priority         ║
║   ⏱️ <0.5s · Pure code                                            ║
║                                                                   ║
║   4. MODEL ROUTER                                                  ║
║   ──────────────                                                   ║
║   Task complexity → Optimal AI model selected:                    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │  COMPLEXITY    → MODEL               CREDITS             │   ║
║   │  ──────────       ─────               ───────             │   ║
║   │  🟢 Quick      → GPT-4o-mini          1-3 cr             │   ║
║   │  🟡 Standard   → Claude Haiku 4.5     3-5 cr              │   ║
║   │  🟠 Deep       → Claude Sonnet 4.6    5-10 cr            │   ║
║   │  🔴 Ultra      → Sonnet 4.6 + Vision  10-20 cr           │   ║
║   │                                                           │   ║
║   │  FALLBACK: 5 failures → auto-switch to next tier         │   ║
║   │  CACHE:    Same pair+TF+style → skip AI, use cached      │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ROUTING RULES:                                                   ║
║   ─────────────                                                    ║
║   • Complex analysis → always Claude Sonnet                        ║
║   • Vision/charts → always Claude Vision                          ║
║   • Code gen → GPT-4o-mini (cheaper)                               ║
║   • Basic explain → Claude Haiku (fast)                           ║
║   • User plan tier can limit model access                         ║
║   ⏱️ <0.1s · Pure code                                           ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │  COMPLEXITY          MODEL TIER       CREDIT COST         │   ║
║   │  ──────────          ──────────       ───────────         │   ║
║   │  🟢 Quick            GPT-4o-mini      1-3 cr             │   ║
║   │  🟡 Standard         Claude Haiku     3-5 cr             │   ║
║   │  🟠 Deep             Claude Sonnet    5-10 cr            │   ║
║   │  🔴 Ultra            Sonnet + Vision  10-20 cr           │   ║
║   │                                                           │   ║
║   │  PRIORITY: 1=Immediate · 2=High · 3=Normal · 4=Low      │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   TASK → AGENT MAPPING:                                            ║
║   analyze → Market Analyst + Bias + Structure + Volatility       ║
║   signal  → Signal + Validation + Risk + Confidence              ║
║   educate → Education + Knowledge + Chart Explanation            ║
║   journal → Journal + Analytics + Psychology                      ║
║   scan    → Screener + Bias + Pattern (all pairs)                ║
║   ⏱️ <0.5s · Pure code                                           ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │  "Analisa XAUUSD H4"                                      │   ║
║   │    → intent: analyze · pair: XAUUSD · tf: H4 · style: ?  │   ║
║   │                                                           │   ║
║   │  "Kenapa market turun padahal NFP bagus?"                 │   ║
║   │    → intent: explain · complexity: medium                 │   ║
║   │                                                           │   ║
║   │  "Backtest strategi OB+FVG 3 bulan"                       │   ║
║   │    → intent: backtest · strategy: OB+FVG · period: 3mo    │   ║
║   │                                                           │   ║
║   │  "Cek psikologi gua minggu ini"                            │   ║
║   │    → intent: psychology · period: week                     │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   5. TASK ANALYSIS                                                 ║
║   ──────────────                                                   ║
║   Orchestrator parses request → determines:                       ║
║   • Intent (analyze / signal / journal / educate / scan)         ║
║   • Complexity (quick / standard / deep)                          ║
║   • Required agents (who needs to work on this?)                 ║
║   • Dependencies (what needs to finish first?)                    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   6. AI AGENTS EXECUTE                                             ║
║   ─────────────────                                                ║
║   All required agents run in parallel:                             ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │  ⭐ Market Analyst      → Full analysis pipeline          │   ║
║   │  🧭 Bias Engine         → 4-layer directional scoring     │   ║
║   │  🏗️ Structure Detection → SMC/ICT narrative               │   ║
║   │  📊 Volatility Agent    → Market temperature              │   ║
║   │  🔮 Pattern Agent       → Chart + candle patterns         │   ║
║   │  🛡️ Risk Agent          → Risk score + lot calc           │   ║
║   │  📡 Data Agent          → Live MT5 + calendar fetch       │   ║
║   │  📚 Knowledge Agent     → RAG vector DB search            │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   Each agent: fetches data → calls tools → returns JSON           ║
║   ⏱️ 5-60s depending on complexity + model                        ║
║                                                                   ║
║   7. RESULT AGGREGATION                                            ║
║   ────────────────────                                             ║
║   All agent results collected → Orchestrator merges               ║
║                                                                   ║
║   8. VALIDATION                                                    ║
║   ────────────                                                     ║
║   Quality check before delivery:                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │  ✅ Consistency    — Do all agents agree?                 │   ║
║   │  ✅ Risk Rules     — Is RR valid? DD within limit?       │   ║
║   │  ✅ Confidence     — Does score meet threshold?           │   ║
║   │  ✅ No Conflicts   — Any contradictory signals?          │   ║
║   │  ✅ Format Check   — Is JSON valid? All fields present?  │   ║
║   │                                                        │   ║
║   │  Pass → Deliver     Fail → Flag + retry/skip             │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║   ⏱️ <1s · Pure code                                              ║
║                                                                   ║
║   9. RESPONSE DELIVERY                                             ║
║   ───────────────────                                              ║
║   Synthesized → Formatted → SSE Streamed → Cached → Logged        ║
║   → Credits deducted                                               ║
║                                                                   ║
║   10. FINAL RESPONSE                                                ║
║   ────────────────                                                 ║
║   User receives complete analysis:                                 ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │  📊 OBSERVATION    — Price action + structure            │   ║
║   │  🧠 REASONING      — Why this trade makes sense          │   ║
║   │  📋 TRADING PLAN   — Entry · SL · TP1/2/3 · RR          │   ║
║   │  ⚠️ RISK           — Lot · Max loss · Rules check        │   ║
║   │  🎯 CONFIDENCE     — GO / CAUTION / NO-GO                │   ║
║   │  ⏰ VALIDITY        — Signal expires in 24h               │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ⏱️ TOTAL: 40-70s (AI-heavy) / 2-5s (cached)                    ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🛡️ Health & Auto-Recovery

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ORCHESTRATOR HEALTH SCAN (Every 30 seconds)                     ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │ SERVICE      │ HEALTH CHECK                               │    ║
║   ├──────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤    ║
║   │ Gateway      │ GET :8000/health                          │    ║
║   │ Terminal     │ GET :8085/health                          │    ║
║   │ Agent Engine │ GET :9003/health                          │    ║
║   │ Signal       │ GET :8106/health                          │    ║
║   │ Risk         │ GET :8105/health                          │    ║
║   │ SMC          │ GET :8006/health                          │    ║
║   │ Indicator    │ GET :8203/health                          │    ║
║   │ Journal      │ GET :8107/health                          │    ║
║   │ MT5 WS       │ GET :8110/health                          │    ║
║   │ Realtime     │ GET :8111/health                          │    ║
║   │ ...          │ (all 40+ services)                         │    ║
║   └──────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   AUTO-RECOVERY PROTOCOL:                                          ║
║   ──────────────────────                                           ║
║   ❌ Service fails health check                                    ║
║        │                                                          ║
║        ├──► 1st fail: Log + retry in 5s                           ║
║        ├──► 2nd fail: docker restart <service>                    ║
║        ├──► 3rd fail: Alert admin via Telegram                    ║
║        └──► Service recovers → Log recovery time                   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   STATUS: ✅ All services healthy · Uptime: 99.8% · Last incident: 3d ago  ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

║   │   fundamentals, and structure into one analysis."        │    ║

║   Risk Agent · Signal Agent · Validation Agent                    ║

║   Structure Detection · Volatility · Pattern · Confirmation       ║
║   Education · Chart Explanation · Journal · Analytics             ║
║                                                                   ║

║   Market Learning · Notify · Knowledge · All DevOps/Security     ║

## 🔄 Agent Communication Protocol

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   How agents talk to each other                                   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   DIRECT (Tool Call):                                              ║
║   ─────────────────                                                ║
║   Agent A → call_api(Agent B) → direct response                   ║
║   Used for: synchronous, need immediate result                    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   EVENT BUS (Redis Streams):                                       ║
║   ─────────────────────────                                       ║
║   Agent A → publish(event) → all subscribers receive              ║
║   Used for: async, broadcast, fire-and-forget                     ║
║                                                                   ║
║   QUEUE (Redis List):                                              ║
║   ─────────────────                                               ║
║   Agent A → LPUSH(task) → Agent B → BRPOP(task)                   ║
║   Used for: ordered processing, load balancing                    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   SHARED MEMORY (Redis Cache):                                     ║
║   ───────────────────────────                                     ║
║   Agent A → cache_set(key, value) → Agent B → cache_get(key)     ║
║   Used for: shared state, results caching                         ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

# 1. ⭐ MARKET ANALYST AGENT

> **"Chief Analyst. The most-used agent in the ecosystem."**

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   DIVISION:   WIN 3 (Trading)                                    ║
║   PRIORITY:   🔴 CRITICAL                                        ║
║   STATUS:     Always ready                                       ║
║                                                                   ║
╠═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                   ║
║   📛 ROLE                                                          ║
║   ────                                                             ║
║   "I combine technicals, fundamentals, sentiment, and structure   ║
║    into ONE clear, actionable analysis. I don't guess.            ║
║    I synthesize data from 8+ engines into a trading plan."        ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📋 FUNCTIONS                                                      ║
║   ──────────                                                       ║
║   📈 TREND ANALYSIS                                                ║
║   ──────────────                                                   ║
║   • Multi-TF trend direction (4 timeframes aligned)              ║
║   • Trend strength (ADX, EMA spacing, swing structure)          ║
║   • Trend phase (impulse / correction / accumulation)           ║
║   • Key swing points (HH, HL, LH, LL)                            ║
║   • BOS/CHOCH detection + invalidation levels                    ║
║   • EMA alignment check (8 > 21 > 50 = bullish)                 ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📐 SNR (SUPPORT & RESISTANCE)                                    ║
║   ────────────────────────────                                     ║
║   • Horizontal S/R (daily, weekly, monthly key levels)          ║
║   • Dynamic S/R (EMA 50/200, trendlines, channels)              ║
║   • SMC zones: Order Blocks, FVG, Breaker, Mitigation           ║
║   • Fibonacci levels (0.382, 0.5, 0.618, 0.786)                ║
║   • Round numbers + psychological levels                        ║
║   • Previous Day/Week/Month High & Low                           ║
║   • Session range S/R (Asian high/low, London open)            ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🏗️ BOS/CHOCH (STRUCTURE BREAKS)                                  ║
║   ──────────────────────────────                                   ║
║   • BOS (Break of Structure) — Trend continuation               ║
║   • CHOCH (Change of Character) — Potential reversal            ║
║   • Multi-TF BOS/CHOCH alignment (D1→H4→H1→M15)                ║
║   • False break detection (wick vs body close)                   ║
║   • Invalidation level auto-calculated                           ║
║   • BOS/CHOCH confirmation rules (candle close + next candle)   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📦 OB/FVG (ORDER BLOCKS & FAIR VALUE GAPS)                      ║
║   ─────────────────────────────────────────                        ║
║   • OB detection — Last bullish/bearish candle before impulse   ║
║   • FVG detection — Unfilled 3-candle imbalance                 ║
║   • OB/FVG confluence scoring (both at same zone = stronger)    ║
║   • OB types: Breaker · Mitigation · Rejection · Unmitigated    ║
║   • FVG fill probability (time elapsed + volatility factor)     ║
║   • Premium/Discount positioning vs dealing range               ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🏛️ MARKET STRUCTURE                                              ║
║   ─────────────────                                               ║
║   • Wyckoff phases: Accumulation · Markup · Distribution · ↓    ║
║   • Market cycle position (early / mid / late trend)            ║
║   • Structural pivot points (where trend changed before)        ║
║   • Multi-TF structural harmony check                            ║
║   • Higher time frame narrative (D1 story vs M15 execution)     ║
║   • Structure-based target projection                            ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📋 TASKS                                                         ║
║   ─────                                                            ║
║   • Full multi-TF analysis (4 timeframes, top-down)              ║
║   • SMC/ICT structure breakdown (OB, FVG, Liq, BOS)             ║
║   • 50+ indicator computation + interpretation                   ║
║   • Pattern detection + validation                                ║
║   • Macro context integration (news, rates, sentiment)           ║
║   • Bias generation with confidence scoring                      ║
║   • Trading plan formulation (Entry, SL, TP, RR)                 ║
║   • Risk validation against user rules + prop firm               ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔧 TOOLS                                                         ║
║   ─────                                                            ║
║   fetch_mt5_data · fetch_chart_screenshot                          ║
║   call_smc_engine · call_indicator_engine                         ║
║   call_pattern_detector · call_regime_detector                    ║
║   call_calendar · call_fundamental · call_sentiment               ║
║   call_correlation · call_risk_engine                              ║
║   search_rag_macro · search_rag_technical                          ║
║   cache_get / cache_set                                            ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔄 WORKFLOW                                                      ║
║   ────────                                                         ║
║   1. Gather Context (parallel)   → MT5 + Calendar + Sentiment    ║
║   2. Technical Layer (parallel)  → SMC + Indicators + Patterns   ║
║   3. Macro Layer (parallel)      → Fundamental + RAG + Correl    ║
║   4. AI Synthesis                → Claude Sonnet 4.6 reasoning   ║
║   5. Output + Cache              → Format JSON → Cache Redis     ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📤 OUTPUT                                                        ║
║   ──────                                                           ║
║   {                                                               ║
║     "observation":    { price_action, structure, key_levels },    ║
║     "reasoning":      { bias, confluences, logic },              ║
║     "trading_plan":   { entry, sl, tp1, tp2, tp3, rr },         ║
║     "risk":           { lot, max_loss, rules_check },            ║
║     "bias":           { direction, confidence, grade }            ║
║   }                                                               ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ⚙️ CONFIG                                                         ║
║   ──────                                                            ║
║   Model:   Claude Sonnet 4.6 (primary) · GPT-4o-mini (fast)     ║
║   Timeout: 120s                                                    ║
║   Retries: 2                                                       ║
║   Cache:   TTL 60s (pair + TF + style)                           ║
║                                                                   ║
║   💰 COST                                                           ║
║   ────                                                             ║
║   Per call: $0.090 (vision included)                              ║
║   Per call (cached): $0.000 (skip AI, return from Redis)         ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```
