# 2. 🎯 SIGNAL AGENT

> **"Trade Plan Generator. From analysis to actionable setup."**

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   DIVISION:   WIN 3 (Trading)                                    ║
║   PRIORITY:   🔴 CRITICAL                                        ║
║   STATUS:     Always ready                                       ║
║                                                                   ║
╠═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                   ║
║   📛 ROLE                                                          ║
║   ────                                                             ║
║   "I take the Market Analyst's observation and turn it into       ║
║    a complete, actionable trading plan. Entry, SL, TP, lot        ║
║    size, risk score, confidence grade — I generate it all."       ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📋 FUNCTIONS                                                     ║
║   ──────────                                                      ║
║   🎯 GENERATE SETUP                                                ║
║   ──────────────                                                   ║
║   • Convert analysis → structured trade setup                     ║
║   • Define entry trigger (limit / market / stop)                  ║
║   • Set invalidation level + re-entry rules                       ║
║   • Partial close strategy (TP1→50%, TP2→30%, TP3→20%)          ║
║   • Move-to-breakeven trigger point                                ║
║   • Time-based exit rules (kill zone close, session end)         ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🎯 SIGNAL GENERATION                                             ║
║   ─────────────────                                               ║
║   • Generate complete signal card from analysis data              ║
║   • Entry zone calculation (OB retest, FVG fill, S/R flip)      ║
║   • SL placement (below structure, beyond sweep, ATR-based)     ║
║   • TP targets (1:2, 1:3, 1:5 based on style)                   ║
║   • Position sizing (balance × risk% × SL distance)              ║
║   • Multi-target TP (TP1 50%, TP2 30%, TP3 20%)                 ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🏅 SIGNAL GRADING                                                ║
║   ──────────────                                                   ║
║   • A+ (80-100%) → LIVE · A (70-79%) → LIVE                      ║
║   • B (55-69%) → WAIT · C (<55%) → FILTER · REJECT → DROP       ║
║   • Grade inputs: Bias score + TF alignment + AI validation      ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🚀 DETECT BREAKOUT                                                ║
║   ────────────────                                                 ║
║   • Range breakout detection (Asian range, session range)        ║
║   • BB squeeze → expansion breakout signal                        ║
║   • Volume surge confirmation (2x+ average volume)               ║
║   • False breakout filter (wick vs body, retest check)           ║
║   • Breakout direction bias (structure + trend alignment)        ║
║   • Auto-SL placement (beyond breakout candle or range)          ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔔 CREATE ALERTS                                                  ║
║   ──────────────                                                   ║
║   • Auto-create alert for signal entry zone reached               ║
║   • TP hit alert + partial close notification                     ║
║   • SL risk alert (price approaching SL)                           ║
║   • Move-to-BE alert (breakeven reached)                           ║
║   • Signal expiry alert (validity ending)                          ║
║   • Multi-channel: Push · Telegram · Email · In-app               ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📊 RISK CALCULATION                                              ║
║   ─────────────────                                                ║
║   • Lot size per $1K balance                                       ║
║   • Max loss check (daily DD limit)                               ║
║   • RR validation (must meet style minimum)                       ║
║   • Prop firm rules check (if enabled)                            ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔧 TOOLS                                                         ║
║   ─────                                                            ║
║   call_risk_engine · calculate_position_size                      ║
║   validate_rr · check_daily_limit · grade_signal                  ║
║   send_alert · cache_set (signal)                                  ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📤 OUTPUT                                                        ║
║   ──────                                                           ║
║   {                                                               ║
║     "signal_card":  { entry, sl, tp1, tp2, tp3, rr, lot },       ║
║     "grade":        "A+",                                          ║
║     "confidence":   85,                                            ║
║     "risk_score":   95,                                            ║
║     "decision":     "GO",                                          ║
║     "validity":     "24 hours"                                     ║
║   }                                                               ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ⚙️ CONFIG                                                         ║
║   ──────                                                            ║
║   Model:   GPT-4o-mini (fast) · Claude Sonnet 4.6 (deep)        ║
║   Timeout: 15s                                                     ║
║   Retries: 1                                                       ║
║                                                                   ║
║   💰 COST                                                           ║

# 3. 🛡️ RISK AGENT

> **"Capital Guardian. Protect first, profit second."**

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   DIVISION:   WIN 3 (Trading)                                    ║
║   PRIORITY:   🔴 CRITICAL                                        ║
║   STATUS:     Always active (every signal goes through me)       ║
║                                                                   ║
╠═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                   ║
║   📛 ROLE                                                          ║
║   ────                                                             ║
║   "I am the last line of defense. Before any signal reaches      ║
║    the trader, I validate every risk parameter. If it doesn't    ║
║    protect capital, I block it. My job is to keep traders        ║
║    alive long enough to become profitable."                      ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📋 FUNCTIONS                                                     ║
║   ──────────                                                      ║
║   🎯 SL/TP VALIDATION                                               ║
║   ─────────────────                                                ║
║   • SL must be behind valid structure (OB, FVG, swing low/high) ║
║   • SL > spread × 3 (prevents spread stop-outs)                 ║
║   • SL < ATR × 2 (reasonable risk distance)                     ║
║   • TP at logical targets (next OB, liq level, Fib extension)  ║
║   • TP RR meets style minimum (scalp 1:1.5, intra 1:2, etc)   ║
║   • Reject if SL behind no structure or TP unrealistic          ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📐 RR CALCULATION                                                ║
║   ────────────────                                                ║
║   • Auto RR calculation (SL distance / TP distance)             ║

║   • Style minimum RR validation (scalp>1:1.5, intra>1:2, etc)  ║
║   • RR-based position scoring (higher RR = higher grade)        ║
║   • Dynamic RR suggestion based on ATR + structure              ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ⚠️ RISK SCORING                                                  ║
║   ──────────────                                                   ║
║   • 6-factor risk score (RR, spread, news, vol, DD, session)    ║
║   • Risk level: 🟢 Low · 🟡 Med · 🟠 High · 🔴 Extreme          ║

║   • Auto-lock on approaching breach (90% of limit → block)      ║

║                                                                   ║

# 6. 📓 JOURNAL AGENT

> **"Your Trading Ledger. Auto-capture. Auto-analyze. Auto-grow."**

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   DIVISION:   WIN 3 (Trading) · WIN 4 (Platform)                 ║
║   PRIORITY:   🟡 HIGH                                             ║
║   STATUS:     Always listening (auto-capture on every trade)     ║
║                                                                   ║
╠═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                   ║
║   📛 ROLE                                                          ║
║   ────                                                             ║
║   "I capture every trade automatically. No copy-paste.            ║
║    No Excel. I know your win rate, your best setup, your worst   ║
║    emotion, and I'll tell you exactly what to improve.            ║
║    The journal is not a chore — it's your edge detector."        ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📋 FUNCTIONS                                                     ║
║   ──────────                                                      ║
║   🧬 PERFORMANCE CLUSTERING                                         ║
║   ────────────────────────                                         ║
║   • Auto-group trades by similarity (setup × session × emotion)  ║
║   • Best cluster: "SMC + London + Calm = 78% WR, +$4,200"       ║
║   • Worst cluster: "Breakout + NY + FOMO = 18% WR, -$1,800"     ║
║   • Optimal trading formula: AI finds YOUR winning combination   ║
║   • Cluster evolution over time (is your edge improving?)        ║
║   • Recommendation: "Trade SMC setups in London only. Skip NY."  ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔍 DETECT BAD HABITS                                              ║
║   ─────────────────                                                ║
║   • Revenge trading: large size after loss + quick re-entry      ║
║   • Overtrading: >5 trades/day with declining win rate          ║
║   • Cutting winners: TP not reached, manual close at <50%       ║
║   • Moving SL: SL widened after entry (>2x original distance)   ║
║   • FOMO entries: entering without signal confirmation          ║
║   • Session addiction: trading outside profitable sessions      ║
║   • Alert: "You've done this 8 times this month. Fix this."    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📈 ANALYZE TRADE HISTORY                                          ║
║   ──────────────────────                                           ║
║   • Win rate by: pair · session · day · setup · emotion          ║
║   • Profit factor + Sharpe ratio over time                       ║
║   • Equity curve with drawdown overlay                            ║
║   • Consecutive win/loss streaks                                   ║
║   • Average holding time (are you cutting winners early?)        ║
║   • Best/worst performing month, week, day                        ║
║   • Compare: this month vs last month vs 3-month average         ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📥 AUTO-CAPTURE                                                  ║
║   ─────────────                                                    ║
║   • MT5 trade detection → auto-create journal entry              ║
║   • Entry: time, price, direction, lot, pair                     ║
║   • Exit: time, price, P&L (pips + USD), duration                ║
║   • Auto-attach chart screenshots (entry + exit)                 ║
║   • Link to source signal (if from Signal Engine)                ║
║   • Manual entry: "/journal XAUUSD buy +50 pips"                ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🏷️ TRADE TAGGING                                                 ║
║   ──────────────                                                   ║
║   • Setup tag: SMC/ICT · Breakout · S/R Flip · Trend · Scalp   ║
║   • Emotion tag: 😊 Calm · 😰 FOMO · 😤 Revenge · 😎 Confident  ║
║   • Mistake tag: ❌ No SL · Oversize · Early exit · Chased       ║
║   • Session tag: Asian · London · NY · Overlap                   ║
║   • AI auto-suggests tags based on trade behavior                ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📊 PATTERN DETECTION                                             ║
║   ─────────────────                                                ║
║   • Winning trade patterns: "You win 71% with SMC setups"        ║
║   • Losing trade patterns: "You lose 80% when no SL used"       ║
║   • Emotion impact: "Calm = +$3,240 · FOMO = -$1,120"          ║
║   • Session analysis: "London 68% · NY 55% · Asian 38%"        ║
║   • Time-based: "You overtrade 13:00-15:00 GMT (lunch dip)"    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔧 TOOLS                                                         ║
║   ─────                                                            ║
║   detect_trade_mt5 · create_journal_entry · attach_screenshot     ║
║   auto_tag_setup · prompt_emotion · detect_patterns               ║
║   link_signal · calculate_metrics                                  ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📤 OUTPUT                                                        ║
║   ──────                                                           ║
║   {                                                               ║
║     "trade":    { entry, exit, pnl, duration, pair },             ║
║     "tags":     { setup, emotion, mistakes, session },           ║
║     "insights": { patterns, strengths, weaknesses },              ║
║     "metrics":  { win_rate, avg_rr, profit_factor }              ║
║   }                                                               ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ⚙️ CONFIG                                                         ║
║   ──────                                                            ║
║   Model:   Claude Haiku 4.5 (tagging + pattern detection)        ║
║           Pure code (auto-capture, metrics)                       ║
║                                                                   ║
║   💰 COST                                                           ║
║   ────                                                             ║
║   Per trade: $0.004 (AI tagging + pattern update)                 ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

# 7. 🔀 ROUTER AGENT

> **"Traffic Director. Every question finds its answer."**

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   DIVISION:   WIN 0 (Orchestrator)                               ║
║   PRIORITY:   🔴 CRITICAL                                        ║
║   STATUS:     Always active (first agent every request hits)     ║
║                                                                   ║
╠═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                   ║
║   📛 ROLE                                                          ║
║   ────                                                             ║
║   "I am the first agent every user request touches. I read       ║
║    their message, understand their intent, and route them to     ║
║    the correct specialist agent. I make sure no request gets     ║
║    lost and every question gets the best possible answer."       ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📋 FUNCTIONS                                                     ║
║   ──────────                                                      ║
║   🔍 INTENT DETECTION                                              ║
║   ─────────────────                                                ║
║   • Natural language parsing → 10 intent types                   ║
║   • Context awareness (previous messages, user level)            ║
║   • Ambiguity resolution ("XAUUSD" = analyze or price check?)   ║
║   • Pair extraction ("analisa gold" → XAUUSD)                    ║
║   • Style detection ("scalping" / "intraday" / "swing")         ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔀 AGENT ROUTING                                                 ║
║   ─────────────                                                    ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │  analyze  → Market Analyst + Bias + Structure + Macro    │   ║
║   │  signal   → Signal Agent + Risk Agent                    │   ║
║   │  educate  → Education Agent + Chart Explanation          │   ║
║   │  journal  → Journal Agent + Analytics                    │   ║
║   │  backtest → Strategy Agent + Backtest Engine             │   ║
║   │  scan     → Screener + Bias Engine (all pairs)           │   ║
║   │  mentor   → Mentor Agent (1-on-1 coaching)               │   ║
║   │  risk     → Risk Agent (position check)                  │   ║
║   │  explain  → Q&A Agent (knowledge base)                   │   ║
║   │  code     → Code Generation (Pine Script / MQL)          │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🧠 CHOOSE BEST AI MODEL                                           ║
║   ─────────────────────                                            ║
║   • Task analysis → optimal model selection in real-time         ║
║   • Cost vs quality trade-off (deep task? use Sonnet, not Haiku) ║
║   • Latency optimization (simple? skip Sonnet, use GPT-4o-mini) ║
║   • Availability check (is primary model up? circuit breaker?)  ║
║   • User preference override (always use Claude / cheapest)      ║
║   • Multi-model routing (parallel calls to 2 models, pick best)  ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📊 MODEL SELECTION                                               ║
║   ────────────────                                                ║
║   • Complexity → Model mapping (quick/standard/deep/ultra)      ║
║   • User plan tier → Model access check                          ║
║   • Credit cost estimation before execution                      ║
║   • Fallback chain (Sonnet → GPT-4o → Haiku)                    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔧 TOOLS                                                         ║
║   ─────                                                            ║
║   detect_intent · extract_pair · detect_style                     ║
║   route_agent · select_model · estimate_cost                      ║
║   health_check (target agent)                                     ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📤 OUTPUT                                                        ║
║   ──────                                                           ║
║   {                                                               ║
║     "intent":       "analyze",                                    ║
║     "pair":         "XAUUSD",                                      ║
║     "style":        "intraday",                                    ║
║     "complexity":   "deep",                                        ║
║     "agents":       ["market_analyst", "bias", "structure"],     ║
║     "model":        "claude-sonnet-4-6",                          ║
║     "estimated_cost": 0.090,                                       ║
║     "estimated_time": "60-90s"                                     ║
║   }                                                               ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ⚙️ CONFIG                                                         ║
║   ──────                                                            ║
║   Model:   GPT-4o-mini (intent + routing)                        ║
║   Timeout: 2s                                                       ║
║                                                                   ║
║   💰 COST                                                           ║
║   ────                                                             ║
║   Per request: $0.001 (light AI call)                              ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🎯 Model Fleet

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   🟢 GPT FAMILY (OpenAI)                                            ║

║   ┌──────────────────┬──────────┬────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │ MODEL            │ STRENGTH │ BEST FOR                    │   ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────────┼────────────────────────────┤   ║
║   │ GPT-4o           │ 🧠 Deep  │ Complex analysis, strategy │   ║
║   │ GPT-4o-mini      │ ⚡ Fast  │ Quick tasks, code gen      │   ║
║   │ GPT-4o Vision    │ 👁️ Vision│ Chart reading, screenshots  │   ║
║   │ GPT-4.1          │ 🧠 Deep  │ Latest, most capable       │   ║

║   │ Claude Sonnet 4.6│ 🧠 Deep  │ Primary analysis, vision   │   ║
║   │ Claude Haiku 4.5 │ ⚡ Fast  │ Tagging, grading, summaries│   ║
║   │ Claude Opus 4.5  │ 🧠 Ultra │ Most complex, multi-step   │   ║
║   └──────────────────┴──────────┴────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔵 GEMINI FAMILY (Google)                                         ║
║   ────────────────────────                                         ║

║   │ Gemini 2.5 Flash │ ⚡ Fast  │ Quick data, summaries      │   ║
║   │ Gemini 3 Flash   │ ⚡ Ultra │ Latest fast model          │   ║
║   │ Gemini 3 Pro     │ 🧠 Ultra │ Complex multi-modal        │   ║
║   └──────────────────┴──────────┴────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🟠 DEEPSEEK FAMILY                                                ║
║   ─────────────────                                                ║
║   ┌──────────────────┬──────────┬────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │ DeepSeek R1      │ 🧠 Reason│ Deep reasoning, logic      │   ║
║   │ DeepSeek V3      │ 💰 Budget│ Cost-effective analysis    │   ║
║   │ DeepSeek V3.1    │ 🧠 Deep  │ Latest, improved reasoning │   ║
║   └──────────────────┴──────────┴────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🏗️ Architecture Requirements

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   WITH 16 MODELS, THE ARCHITECTURE MUST HAVE:                     ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔀 UNIFIED API LAYER                                             ║
║   ──────────────────                                               ║
║   • Single interface for all 16 models (OpenAI-compatible)       ║
║   • Standardized request/response format                          ║
║   • Model-agnostic agent code (swap model without code change)   ║
║   • Provider abstraction (Anthropic · OpenAI · OpenRouter)       ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🧠 INTELLIGENT ROUTER                                            ║
║   ──────────────────                                               ║
║   • Task analysis → auto-select optimal model                     ║
║   • Cost/quality/latency trade-off per request                    ║
║   • User plan tier enforcement (limits model access)             ║
║   • Real-time availability tracking (circuit breaker per model)  ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔄 FALLBACK CHAIN                                                ║
║   ────────────────                                                 ║
║   • Primary fails → auto-switch to fallback                       ║
║   • Graceful degradation (Sonnet→GPT→Haiku→DeepSeek)            ║
║   • Circuit breaker: 5 fails → 300s cooldown                      ║
║   • Zero user impact on model failure                             ║
║                                                                   ║
║   💰 COST CONTROL                                                  ║
║   ────────────                                                     ║
║   • Per-model cost tracking + budget alerts                       ║
║   • Credit deduction BEFORE model call                             ║
║   • User-tier based model access                                  ║
║   • Response cache (TTL 60s) → skip AI when possible             ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📊 MONITORING                                                    ║
║   ────────────                                                     ║
║   • Per-model: latency, error rate, cost, usage                   ║
║   • Auto-detection: model quality degradation                     ║
║   • A/B testing: compare model outputs for same task             ║
║   • Weekly model performance report                               ║
║                                                                   ║
║   🔌 HOT-SWAP CAPABILITY                                           ║
║   ────────────────────                                             ║
║   • Add new model → 1 YAML config change                          ║
║   • Remove deprecated model → zero code impact                    ║
║   • Model version pinning (lock to specific version)             ║
║   • A/B test new model vs current before full switch              ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

---

# 🔀 MODEL ROUTER ENGINE

> **"The Brain That Picks THE Brain. 16 Models, 1 Smart Router."**

## 🎯 How It Works

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   TASK INPUT → ROUTER DECISION → OUTPUT                          ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  0. TASK INPUT                                          │    ║
║   │  ────────────                                           │    ║
║   │  "/analyze XAUUSD H4 intraday"                          │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │         ▼                                                │    ║
║   │  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐          │    ║
║   │  │  ROUTER ENGINE                            │          │    ║
║   │  │                                           │          │    ║
║   │  │  1. Intent Detection                       │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Intent: analyze                      │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Pair: XAUUSD · TF: H4                │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Style: intraday                      │          │    ║
║   │  │                                           │          │    ║
║   │  │  2. Complexity Analysis                    │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Depth: 4-TF multi-layered             │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Vision: Required (charts)            │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Reasoning: Deep (why this setup)     │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Level: 🟠 DEEP                       │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Estimated tokens: ~8,000              │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Estimated cost: $0.09-0.25           │          │    ║
║   │  │                                           │          │    ║
║   │  │  3. Task Classification                    │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Intent: analyze                      │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Complexity: 🟠 Deep                  │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Requires: Vision + Reasoning         │          │    ║
║   │  │                                           │          │    ║
║   │  │  4. Cost Analysis                          │          │    ║
║   │  │     • User credits: 350 cr available       │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Task cost range: $0.02 - $0.25       │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Budget tier: Premium (Sonnet access) │          │    ║
║   │  │     • Optimization: Route to Sonnet ($0.09)│          │    ║
║   │  │     • Savings vs Ultra: $0.16 (64% less)   │          │    ║
║   │  │                                           │          │    ║
║   │  │  5. Model Scoring                          │          │    ║
║   │  │     ┌──────────────────┬──────┬──────┐    │          │    ║
║   │  │     │ MODEL            │ COST │FIT % │    │          │    ║
║   │  │     ├──────────────────┼──────┼──────┤    │          │    ║
║   │  │     │ Claude Sonnet 4.6│ $90  │ 98%✅│    │          │    ║
║   │  │     │ GPT-4o           │ $50  │ 85%  │    │          │    ║
║   │  │     │ GPT-4o-mini      │ $1   │ 55%  │    │          │    ║
║   │  │     │ DeepSeek R1      │ $2   │ 70%  │    │          │    ║
║   │  │     │ Gemini 2.5 Pro   │ $25  │ 75%  │    │          │    ║
║   │  │     └──────────────────┴──────┴──────┘    │          │    ║
║   │  │                                           │          │    ║
║   │  │  3. Decision                               │          │    ║
║   │  │     → Claude Sonnet 4.6 (98% fit, $0.09)  │          │    ║
║   │  │     → Fallback: GPT-4o (85% fit, $0.05)   │          │    ║
║   │  │     → Cache check: TTL 60s                 │          │    ║
║   │  └──────────────────────────────────────────┘          │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │         ▼                                                │    ║
║   │  Claude Sonnet 4.6 → Execute → Return                   │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 📊 Scoring Algorithm

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   MODEL_FIT_SCORE = QUALITY × COST_EFFICIENCY × AVAILABILITY     ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  QUALITY (40%):                                         │    ║
║   │  • Task alignment score (can this model do this?)       │    ║
║   │  • Historical performance on similar tasks              │    ║
║   │  • User satisfaction rating                              │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  COST EFFICIENCY (35%):                                  │    ║
║   │  • Cost per 1K tokens                                   │    ║
║   │  • Typical token usage for this task                    │    ║
║   │  • User's remaining credits                              │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  AVAILABILITY (25%):                                     │    ║
║   │  • Circuit breaker status (open/closed)                 │    ║
║   │  • Current latency (p95)                                 │    ║
║   │  • Error rate (last 100 calls)                           │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🔄 Fallback Protocol

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   PRIMARY → FALLBACK 1 → FALLBACK 2 → FALLBACK 3                ║
║                                                                   ║
║   DEEP TASKS:                                                      ║
║   Sonnet 4.6 → GPT-4o → DeepSeek R1 → Haiku (min quality)      ║
║                                                                   ║
║   FAST TASKS:                                                      ║
║   GPT-4o-mini → Haiku 4.5 → Gemini Flash → local cache          ║
║                                                                   ║
║   VISION TASKS:                                                    ║
║   Sonnet Vision → GPT-4o Vision → "No chart available"          ║
║                                                                   ║
║   RULES:                                                           ║
║   ─────                                                            ║
║   • Primary fails → immediate fallback (no retry delay)          ║
║   • 5 failures on primary → circuit breaker OPEN (300s)         ║
║   • Fallback failure → move to next in chain                     ║
║   • All models down → return cached result or error gracefully  ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

# ⚡ ROUTING EXAMPLE

> **"Real Case Study. How the Router picks the perfect model."**

## Example 1: Complex Analysis

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   USER: "/analyze XAUUSD H4 intraday"                            ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  STEP 1: TASK INPUT                                     │    ║
║   │  "/analyze XAUUSD H4 intraday"                          │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │  STEP 2: INTENT DETECTION                                │    ║
║   │  intent=analyze · pair=XAUUSD · tf=H4 · style=intraday  │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │  STEP 3: COMPLEXITY ANALYSIS                             │    ║
║   │  needs_vision=true · depth=deep · tokens=~8K            │    ║
║   │  level=🟠 DEEP                                            │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │  STEP 4: COST ANALYSIS                                   │    ║
║   │  user_plan=premium · credits=350 · budget=$0.09-0.25    │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │  STEP 5: MODEL SCORING                                   │    ║
║   │  ┌──────────────────┬──────────┬──────────┬──────────┐  │    ║
║   │  │ MODEL            │ FIT(40%) │COST(35%) │AVAIL(25%)│  │    ║
║   │  ├──────────────────┼──────────┼──────────┼──────────┤  │    ║
║   │  │ Claude Sonnet 4.6│   98     │   70     │   100    │  │    ║
║   │  │ GPT-4o           │   85     │   85     │   100    │  │    ║
║   │  │ DeepSeek R1      │   70     │   95     │   90     │  │    ║
║   │  │ Gemini 2.5 Pro   │   75     │   80     │   95     │  │    ║
║   │  │ GPT-4o-mini      │   55     │   100    │   100    │  │    ║
║   │  └──────────────────┴──────────┴──────────┴──────────┘  │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │  STEP 6: DECISION                                        │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  🏆 SELECTED: Claude Sonnet 4.6                          │    ║
║   │  Score: 98×0.4 + 70×0.35 + 100×0.25 = 88.7/100         │    ║
║   │  Cost: $0.09  ·  Time: 40-60s  ·  Fallback: GPT-4o      │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  ✅ Anthropic API → SSE Stream → Response → Cache        │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## Example 2: Quick Task

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   USER: "Apa itu FVG dan cara entry-nya?"                        ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  INTENT=educate · COMPLEXITY=🟢 QUICK · TOKENS=~500     │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  MODEL SCORING:                                         │    ║
║   │  ┌──────────────────┬──────────┬──────────┬──────────┐  │    ║
║   │  │ GPT-4o-mini      │   90     │   100    │   100    │  │    ║
║   │  │ Claude Haiku 4.5 │   85     │   90     │   100    │  │    ║
║   │  │ Claude Sonnet    │   98     │   10     │   100    │  │    ║
║   │  └──────────────────┴──────────┴──────────┴──────────┘  │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  🏆 SELECTED: GPT-4o-mini                                │    ║
║   │  Score: 90×0.4 + 100×0.35 + 100×0.25 = 96/100          │    ║
║   │  Cost: $0.001  ·  Time: <2s                               │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  💡 Sonnet CAN do this, but COST is terrible.            │    ║
║   │     Router saved 99% cost with same quality.             │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## Example 3: Fallback in Action

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   USER: "/signal XAUUSD scalping" — but Sonnet is DOWN           ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  PRIMARY: Claude Sonnet 4.6    → ❌ CIRCUIT OPEN        │    ║
║   │  FALLBACK 1: GPT-4o           → ✅ AVAILABLE            │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  Decision: Route to GPT-4o (85% fit, $0.05)             │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  📊 Quality slightly lower (85% vs 98%)                  │    ║
║   │  💰 Cost slightly higher for this tier                   │    ║
║   │  ⚡ But user gets response NOW (not "try again later")   │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  🔄 Sonnet auto-retested in 300s → if recovered,        │    ║
║   │     circuit closes → next request uses Sonnet again     │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 📋 Task → Model Mapping

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────┬──────────────────┬──────────────┐ ║
║   │ TASK                     │ PRIMARY          │ FALLBACK      │ ║
║   ├──────────────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────┤ ║
║   │ Deep Reasoning           │ GPT-4o / o3-mini │ DeepSeek R1   │ ║
║   │ Coding (Pine/MQL/Python) │ Claude Opus 4.5  │ Claude Sonnet │ ║
║   │ Fast Analysis (no vision)│ Gemini 3 Flash   │ GPT-4o-mini   │ ║
║   │ Cheap Mass Analysis      │ DeepSeek V3      │ GPT-4o-mini   │ ║
║   │ Chart Explanation        │ Claude Vision    │ GPT-4o Vision │ ║
║   │ Full Analysis (vision)   │ Claude Sonnet 4.6│ GPT-4o Vision │ ║
║   │ Full Analysis (no vision)│ Claude Sonnet 4.6│ GPT-4o        │ ║
║   │ Signal Generation (full) │ Claude Sonnet 4.6│ GPT-4o        │ ║
║   │ Signal Generation (fast) │ GPT-4o-mini      │ Claude Haiku  │ ║
║   │ Market Structure (SMC)   │ Claude Haiku 4.5 │ GPT-4o-mini   │ ║
║   │ Bias Scoring (4-layer)   │ Claude Haiku 4.5 │ GPT-4o-mini   │ ║
║   │ Risk / Lot Calculation   │ Pure Code        │ —             │ ║
║   │ Education / Q&A (quick)  │ GPT-4o-mini      │ Claude Haiku  │ ║
║   │ Education (deep explain) │ Claude Sonnet 4.6│ GPT-4o        │ ║
║   │ Chart Screenshot (Vision)│ Claude Sonnet 4.6│ GPT-4o Vision │ ║
║   │ Journal Tagging          │ Claude Haiku 4.5 │ GPT-4o-mini   │ ║
║   │ Journal Pattern Detection│ Pure Code        │ GPT-4o-mini   │ ║
║   │ Strategy Builder         │ Claude Sonnet 4.6│ GPT-4o        │ ║
║   │ Backtest Engine          │ Gemini 2.5 Pro   │ GPT-4o        │ ║
║   │ Screener (20+ pairs)     │ GPT-4o-mini      │ Claude Haiku  │ ║
║   │ Psychology Check         │ Pure Code        │ GPT-4o-mini   │ ║
║   │ Mentor Coaching          │ Claude Sonnet 4.6│ GPT-4o        │ ║
║   │ Code Gen (Pine/MQL)      │ GPT-4o-mini      │ Claude Haiku  │ ║
║   │ Intent Detection         │ GPT-4o-mini      │ Rule-based    │ ║
║   │ Macro Analysis           │ GPT-4o-mini      │ Claude Haiku  │ ║
║   │ Embedding (RAG)          │ text-embed-3     │ —             │ ║
║   └──────────────────────────┴──────────────────┴──────────────┘ ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 💰 Cost Per Task

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────┬──────────┬──────────┬────────────┐ ║
║   │ TASK                     │ MODEL    │ COST     │ CREDITS    │ ║
║   ├──────────────────────────┼──────────┼──────────┼────────────┤ ║
║   │ Full Analysis (vision)   │ Sonnet   │ $0.090   │ 10 cr      │ ║
║   │ Full Analysis (no vision)│ Sonnet   │ $0.060   │ 7 cr       │ ║
║   │ Signal Generation (full) │ Mixed    │ $0.099   │ 11 cr      │ ║
║   │ Signal (fast)            │ GPT-mini │ $0.003   │ 3 cr       │ ║
║   │ Bias + Structure         │ Haiku    │ $0.009   │ 3 cr       │ ║
║   │ Chart Explanation        │ Sonnet V │ $0.015   │ 5 cr       │ ║
║   │ Education Q&A (quick)    │ GPT-mini │ $0.001   │ 1 cr       │ ║
║   │ Education (deep)         │ Sonnet   │ $0.012   │ 5 cr       │ ║
║   │ Strategy Builder         │ Sonnet   │ $0.025   │ 8 cr       │ ║
║   │ Backtest                 │ Gemini   │ $0.040   │ 20 cr      │ ║
║   │ Screener (20 pairs)      │ GPT-mini │ $0.005   │ 15 cr      │ ║
║   │ Mentor Session           │ Sonnet   │ $0.012   │ 10 cr      │ ║
║   │ Journal AI               │ Haiku    │ $0.004   │ 2 cr       │ ║
║   │ Macro Report             │ GPT-mini │ $0.002   │ 2 cr       │ ║
║   │ Risk / Psych / Metrics   │ Code     │ $0.000   │ 1 cr       │ ║
║   │ Embedding (RAG)          │ Embed    │ $0.001   │ 1 cr       │ ║
║   └──────────────────────────┴──────────┴──────────┴────────────┘ ║
║                                                                   ║
║   1 credit = $0.009                                               ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

# 🔥 PROVIDER ARCHITECTURE

> **"Multi-Provider. One Interface. Zero Lock-In."**

## 🏢 AI Provider Map

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                    GAS UNIFIED API                        │    ║
║   │              Single Interface for ALL Providers          │    ║
║   └────────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                            │                                      ║
║                    ┌───────┴───────┐                             ║
║                    │   🔀 AI       │                             ║
║                    │   ROUTER     │                             ║
║                    │  Task→Model  │                             ║
║                    │  Model→Prov  │                             ║
║                    │  Cost Optim  │                             ║
║                    │  Fallback    │                             ║
║                    └───────┬───────┘                             ║
║                            │                                      ║
║     ┌──────────┬───────────┼───────────┬──────────┐             ║
║     │          │           │           │          │             ║
║     ▼          ▼           ▼           ▼          ▼             ║
║  ┌──────┐ ┌──────┐   ┌──────┐   ┌──────┐   ┌──────────┐       ║
║  │ ANTH │ │OPENAI│   │GOOGLE│   │ OPEN │   │ LOCALHOST │       ║
║  │ROPIC │ │      │   │      │   │ROUTER│   │ (Ollama)  │       ║
║  ├──────┤ ├──────┤   ├──────┤   ├──────┤   ├──────────┤       ║
║  │Sonnet│ │GPT-4o│   │Gemini│   │Deep- │   │ Llama    │       ║
║  │Haiku │ │GPT-4o│   │ 2.5  │   │ Seek │   │ Mistral  │       ║
║  │Opus  │ │ -mini│   │ Pro  │   │ Kimi │   │ Qwen     │       ║
║  │      │ │o3-min│   │Flash │   │ Grok │   │ Custom   │       ║
║  │      │ │embed │   │      │   │ GLM  │   │          │       ║
║  └──────┘ └──────┘   └──────┘   └──────┘   └──────────┘       ║
║                                                                   ║
║  DIRECT API:          Anthropic · OpenAI · Google                 ║
║  VIA OPENROUTER:      DeepSeek · Kimi · Grok · GLM · Qwen        ║
║  LOCAL:               Ollama (Llama, Mistral, Custom)             ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🔌 Provider Adapters

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   🔀 AI ROUTER                                                     ║
║   ├── 🟢 OpenAI Adapter                                           ║
║   │   Models: GPT-4o · GPT-4o-mini · o3-mini · Embeddings       ║
║   │   Auth:   API Key (Bearer token)                             ║
║   │   Format: Native (OpenAI-compatible)                          ║
║   │   Features: Vision · Streaming · Function Calling · JSON     ║
║   │                                                               ║
║   ├── 🟣 Anthropic Adapter                                        ║
║   │   Models: Sonnet 4.6 · Haiku 4.5 · Opus 4.5                 ║
║   │   Auth:   API Key (x-api-key header)                         ║
║   │   Format: Anthropic Messages API → OpenAI-compatible wrapper  ║
║   │   Features: Vision · Streaming · Extended Thinking           ║
║   │                                                               ║
║   ├── 🔵 Gemini Adapter                                           ║
║   │   Models: 2.5 Pro · 2.5 Flash · 3 Flash · 3 Pro            ║
║   │   Auth:   Service Account / API Key                           ║
║   │   Format: Google GenAI SDK → OpenAI-compatible wrapper       ║
║   │   Features: Vision · Streaming · Long Context (1M+)         ║
║   │                                                               ║
║   ├── 🟠 OpenRouter Adapter                                       ║
║   │   Models: Kimi K2.5 · Grok 4.1 · Qwen 3.5 · GLM 5         ║
║   │   Auth:   API Key (Bearer token)                             ║
║   │   Format: OpenAI-compatible (native)                          ║
║   │   Features: Multi-provider · Cost comparison · Fallback      ║
║   │                                                               ║
║   └── 🟤 DeepSeek Adapter                                          ║
║       Models: DeepSeek R1 · DeepSeek V3 · DeepSeek V3.1        ║
║       Auth:   API Key (Bearer token)                             ║
║       Format: OpenAI-compatible (native)                          ║
║       Features: Deep reasoning · Ultra-low cost · Chain-of-thought║
║   │                                                               ║
║   └── ⚪ Ollama Adapter (Local)                                   ║
║       Models: Llama 3 · Mistral · Qwen · Custom fine-tunes      ║
║       Auth:   None (localhost)                                    ║
║       Format: OpenAI-compatible (Ollama v1)                       ║
║       Features: Zero cost · Zero latency · Full privacy          ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 📦 Unified Response Format

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ALL providers → ONE standard output format                     ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  {                                                      │    ║
║   │    "id": "resp_abc123",                                 │    ║
║   │    "model": "claude-sonnet-4-6",                        │    ║
║   │    "provider": "anthropic",                               │    ║
║   │    "created": 1700000000,                                │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │    "usage": {                                           │    ║
║   │      "prompt_tokens": 8000,                             │    ║
║   │      "completion_tokens": 1500,                          │    ║
║   │      "total_tokens": 9500,                               │    ║
║   │      "cost_usd": 0.090                                 │    ║
║   │    },                                                    │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │    "choices": [{                                         │    ║
║   │      "index": 0,                                         │    ║
║   │      "message": {                                        │    ║
║   │        "role": "assistant",                              │    ║
║   │        "content": "Here is the analysis...",             │    ║
║   │        "tool_calls": []                                  │    ║
║   │      },                                                   │    ║
║   │      "finish_reason": "stop"                             │    ║
║   │    }],                                                   │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │    "gas_metadata": {                                    │    ║
║   │      "routing": {                                       │    ║
║   │        "primary_model": "claude-sonnet-4-6",            │    ║
║   │        "fallback_used": false,                           │    ║
║   │        "cache_hit": false                                │    ║
║   │      },                                                   │    ║
║   │      "timing_ms": {                                      │    ║
║   │        "total": 45000,                                   │    ║
║   │        "model_latency": 42000,                            │    ║
║   │        "routing_latency": 3000                           │    ║
║   │      },                                                   │    ║
║   │      "credits_deducted": 10                              │    ║
║   │    }                                                     │    ║
║   │  }                                                      │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ALL adapters normalize to this format:                          ║
║   Anthropic Messages → OpenAI format                              ║
║   Google GenAI       → OpenAI format                              ║
║   OpenRouter         → Native OpenAI format                       ║
║   DeepSeek           → Native OpenAI format                       ║
║   Ollama             → Native OpenAI format                       ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## ⚡ Easy Model Switch

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   Ganti model = 1 LINE CONFIG. Zero code change.                 ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  # config/models.yaml                                    │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  analysis:                                               │    ║
║   │    primary: claude-sonnet-4-6     # ← ganti ini aja     │    ║
║   │    fallback: gpt-4o                                      │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  # Mau ganti ke GPT-4o?                                  │    ║
║   │  # analysis:                                             │    ║
║   │  #   primary: gpt-4o              # ← 1 line changed    │    ║
║   │  #   fallback: claude-sonnet-4-6                         │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  # Mau tambah model baru?                                 │    ║
║   │  # models:                                               │    ║
║   │  #   - name: gemini-4-flash    # ← 3 lines added        │    ║
║   │  #     provider: google                                  │    ║
║   │  #     tier: fast                                        │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  ALL agent code stays EXACTLY the same.                  │    ║
║   │  Semua agent panggil call_model("analysis", ...)         │    ║
║   │  Router yang handle provider + model di belakang.        │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   SWITCH SCENARIOS:                                                ║
║   ────────────────                                                 ║
║   🔄 Sonnet downtime  →  ganti primary: "gpt-4o" · 1 line       ║
║   💰 Budget cut       →  ganti primary: "deepseek-v3" · 1 line  ║
║   🚀 New model drops  →  tambah 3 lines YAML · langsung pakai   ║
║   🧪 A/B testing      →  primary: [sonnet, gpt4o] · bandingkan  ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 📈 Easy Scaling

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   Scale horizontally. Add providers effortlessly.                ║
║                                                                   ║
║   NEW PROVIDER = 1 ADAPTER FILE + 3 LINES YAML                    ║
║   ─────────────────────────────────────────                        ║
║   • Create adapter class (50 lines)                               ║
║   • Add model to config (3 lines YAML)                            ║
║   • ✅ LIVE — zero agent code change                              ║
║                                                                   ║
║   CONCURRENCY:                                                     ║
║   1→10→100→1000 users — async parallel, auto-scale               ║
║   Each adapter STATELESS → scale infinitely                      ║
║   Redis queue + cache → zero bottleneck                           ║
║                                                                   ║
║   COST SCALING:                                                    ║
║   1 user/day:    ~$0.50   (active trading)                       ║
║   100 users:      ~$50/d  (rev: $1,199/mo Premium)              ║
║   1,000 users:    ~$500/d (rev: $11,990/mo)                      ║
║   10,000 users:   ~$5K/d  (rev: $119,900/mo)                    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   Margin: 85-90% after AI costs                                   ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

# 📡 DATA ARCHITECTURE

> **"The Data Flow. Storage. Caching. Real-Time Streams."**

## 🗄️ Storage Layer

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                    STORAGE STACK                          │    ║
║   ├──────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────────┤    ║
║   │ POSTGRES │ PRIMARY DATABASE                              │    ║
║   │ :5432    │ Users · Analyses · Journals · Backtests       │    ║
║   │          │ Subscriptions · Credits · Signal History      │    ║
║   │          │ Schema: UUID PK · JSONB · Timestamps          │    ║
║   ├──────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────┤    ║
║   │ REDIS    │ CACHE + QUEUE + PUB/SUB                        │    ║
║   │ :6379    │ AI Response Cache (TTL 60s)                   │    ║
║   │          │ Job Queue (Bull/BullMQ pattern)               │    ║
║   │          │ Event Bus (Redis Streams)                      │    ║
║   │          │ Session State (TTL 10min)                      │    ║
║   │          │ Live Prices (TTL 5s, from MT5)                │    ║
║   ├──────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────┤    ║
║   │ MINIO    │ OBJECT STORAGE                                 │    ║
║   │ :9010    │ Chart Screenshots (PNG, 24h retention)        │    ║
║   │          │ ML Models (strategy models, .pkl files)       │    ║
║   │          │ PDF Reports (weekly, monthly)                  │    ║
║   │          │ User Uploads (chart images, documents)        │    ║
║   ├──────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────┤    ║
║   │ CHROMADB │ VECTOR DATABASE                                 │    ║
║   │ :8007    │ RAG Macro (economic concepts, history)        │    ║
║   │          │ RAG Technical (ICT/SMC, price action)         │    ║
║   │          │ Course Content Embeddings                      │    ║
║   │          │ Semantic Search (user Q&A history)            │    ║
║   └──────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🔄 Data Pipeline

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   REAL-TIME DATA FLOW                                             ║
║                                                                   ║
║   MT5 EXNESS (Docker VNC)                                        ║
║        │                                                          ║
║        ├──► Tick Stream (WS :8110)                                ║
║        │       │                                                   ║
║        │       ├──► Redis Streams (real-time, TTL 5s)            ║
║        │       └──► Realtime Hub :8111 → Frontend WS             ║
║        │                                                          ║
║        ├──► OHLC Data (REST :8100)                                ║
║        │       │                                                   ║
║        │       └──► PostgreSQL (M1-MN historical)                 ║
║        │                                                          ║
║        └──► EA v4.0 PRO                                           ║
║               │                                                    ║
║               ├──► Context Push → Gateway :8000                   ║
║               ├──► Order Queue ← Redis (LPUSH/BRPOP)              ║
║               └──► Trade Result → Journal :8107 → PostgreSQL      ║
║                                                                   ║
║   EXTERNAL DATA SOURCES (Polling)                                  ║
║   ──────────────────────────────                                   ║
║   ForexFactory    → Calendar :9601 (every 60s)                    ║
║   CFTC/COT        → Fundamental :9603 (weekly, Friday)           ║
║   Alternative.me  → Sentiment :8009 (every 120s)                  ║
║   DEX Screener    → Memecoin :8213 (every 60s)                    ║
║   PolyMarket API  → PolyMarket :8212 (every 30s)                 ║
║   Binance WS      → Binance :9612 (real-time stream)              ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## ⚡ Caching Strategy

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │ CACHE TYPE          KEY                TTL     HIT RATE  │    ║
║   ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤    ║
║   │ AI Response         ai:{pair}:{tf}:{style}  60s    40-60%│   ║
║   │ Signal Cache        signal:{pair}:{tf}     30s    30-50%│   ║
║   │ Calendar Cache      calendar:{date}        300s   80-90%│   ║
║   │ Sentiment Cache     sentiment:global       120s   70-80%│   ║
║   │ Live Price Cache    price:{symbol}          5s    90-95%│   ║
║   │ User Session        session:{user_id}      600s   100%  ║
║   │ RAG Embeddings      embed:{hash}           24h    60-70%│   ║
║   │ Indicator Results   indicator:{pair}:{tf}   30s   50-60%│   ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   EVICTION: LRU (Least Recently Used) · Max memory: 512MB        ║
║   PERSISTENCE: AOF + RDB (survives restart)                       ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 📊 Data Retention

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │ DATA TYPE      │ RETENTION POLICY                          │  ║
║   ├────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤  ║
║   │ User Accounts  │ Forever (GDPR delete on request)         │  ║
║   │ Trade Journals │ Forever (core asset for analytics)       │  ║
║   │ AI Analyses    │ 90 days (then archived to cold storage)  │  ║
║   │ Signals        │ 90 days (for performance tracking)       │  ║
║   │ Chat History   │ 30 days (rolling window)                  │  ║
║   │ Screenshots    │ 24 hours (MinIO auto-expire)              │  ║
║   │ Live Prices    │ 5 seconds (Redis, real-time only)        │  ║
║   │ OHLC Data      │ 5 years (M1-MN, compressed after 1yr)   │  ║
║   │ Cache Data     │ Auto-expire per TTL                       │  ║
║   │ Logs           │ 7 days (Loki ring buffer)                 │  ║
║   │ Backups        │ Daily (PostgreSQL) · Weekly (MinIO)      │  ║
║   └────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🏗️ MT5 Data Architecture

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   MT5 EXNESS (Docker VNC) — THE KING                             ║
║                                                                   ║

║   │                                                         │    ║

║   │     ┌─────────────────┼─────────────────┐              │    ║
║   │     │                 │                 │              │    ║
║   │     ▼                 ▼                 ▼              │    ║
║   │  ┌────────┐    ┌────────────┐    ┌──────────┐        │    ║

║   │      │               │                │               │    ║
║   └──────┼───────────────┼────────────────┼───────────────┘    ║
║          │               │                │                     ║
║          ▼               ▼                ▼                     ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │                                                         │  ║
║   │  EA v4.0 PRO          MT5 WS :8110     MT5 DATA :8100   │  ║
║   │  ──────────           ────────────     ──────────────    │  ║
║   │  • Context Push       • Tick Stream    • OHLC History   │  ║
║   │  • Order Execution    • Real-time      • M1→MN (5yr)    │  ║
║   │  • Signal Polling     • Bid/Ask/Spread • REST API       │  ║
║   │  • Heartbeat          • < 50ms latency  • Batch Export  │  ║
║   │  • Trade Journal      • Redis Streams   • PostgreSQL    │  ║
║   │  • Risk Rules         • → Realtime Hub  • Compressed    │  ║
║   │                                                         │  ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ⚠️ MT5 IS THE ONLY SOURCE OF:                                   ║
║   ────────────────────────────                                    ║
║   ✅ Live Prices (Bid/Ask/Spread) — from broker, not 3rd party  ║
║   ✅ Tick Data — every price change captured                     ║
║   ✅ OHLC Candles — M1 to MN, complete history                   ║
║   ✅ Account Data — balance, equity, margin, positions           ║
║   ✅ Trade Execution — orders placed, modified, closed           ║
║   ✅ Trade History — every trade, verified by broker             ║
║                                                                   ║
║   BINANCE = SECONDARY (crypto only)                               ║
║   TRADINGVIEW = TERTIARY (chart visualization only)               ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

║   │  MT5 EA   → Context Push → Dashboard (account live)     │   ║

║   │                                                         │   ║

## 📓 5. TRADE HISTORY DATA

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║

║   │ price_close    float     2665.00       Exit price        │    ║

║   │ swap           float     -0.50         Total swap         │    ║
║   │ commission     float     -1.50         Total commission   │    ║
║   │ time_open      int       1700000000    Entry time         │    ║
║   │ time_close     int       1700018000    Exit time          │    ║
║   │ duration_min   int       300           Duration (minutes) │    ║
║   │ sl             float     2640.00       SL when closed    │    ║
║   │ tp             float     2670.00       TP when closed    │    ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║

## 📊 SPREAD MONITOR

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   Real-time spread tracking from MT5 broker                      ║
║                                                                   ║
║   WHY SPREAD MATTERS:                                              ║
║   ─────────────────                                                ║
║   • Real cost of trading (spread × lot size)                      ║
║   • Widens during news → avoid entries                            ║
║   • Different per session (Asian wider, London tighter)          ║
║   • Broker quality indicator                                       ║
║                                                                   ║
║   SPREAD LEVELS (XAUUSD Example):                                  ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │  LEVEL       SPREAD      ACTION                          │   ║
║   │  ─────       ──────      ──────                          │   ║
║   │  🟢 TIGHT    < 1.0 pip   Trade normal size              │   ║
║   │  🟡 NORMAL   1.0-2.0     Trade with caution             │   ║
║   │  🟠 WIDE     2.0-5.0     Reduce size or wait            │   ║
║   │  🔴 EXTREME   > 5.0      DO NOT TRADE (news/rollover)   │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   SPREAD PER PAIR (Average, London Session):                       ║
║   ┌──────────┬──────────┬──────────┬──────────┐                  ║
║   │ PAIR     │ SPREAD   │ PAIR     │ SPREAD   │                  ║
║   ├──────────┼──────────┼──────────┼──────────┤                  ║
║   │ XAUUSD   │ 0.8-1.5  │ EURUSD   │ 0.1-0.3  │                  ║
║   │ GBPUSD   │ 0.3-0.8  │ USDJPY   │ 0.2-0.5  │                  ║
║   │ BTCUSD   │ 15-30    │ US30     │ 1.0-3.0  │                  ║
║   │ XAGUSD   │ 1.0-2.0  │ UK100    │ 1.0-2.0  │                  ║
║   └──────────┴──────────┴──────────┴──────────┘                  ║
║                                                                   ║
║   SPREAD PROTECTION RULES:                                         ║
║   ──────────────────────                                          ║
║   • Spread > 3× normal → auto-downgrade signal                    ║
║   • Spread > 5× normal → block new entries                        ║
║   • News event ±15min → spread warning active                     ║
║   • Rollover (00:00 GMT) → expect wider spreads                   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   SOURCE: MT5 Tick Data (bid-ask difference, real-time)          ║
║   ⏱️ UPDATES: Every tick (<50ms)                                  ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

## 💰 TRADING — Execution Flow

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   SIGNAL → ORDER → EXECUTION → JOURNAL → ANALYTICS               ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  1. SIGNAL GENERATED                                     │    ║
║   │  ────────────────                                        │    ║
║   │  AI / Pine Script generates structured trade signal:     │    ║
║   │  { pair, direction, entry, sl, tp1, tp2, tp3, rr, lot } │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │         ▼                                                │    ║
║   │  2. TRADER REVIEWS                                        │    ║
║   │  ────────────────                                         │    ║
║   │  Reviews signal card on Dashboard/Chat:                   │    ║
║   │  • Entry zone + SL + TP levels                            │    ║
║   │  • Risk score + confidence grade                          │    ║
║   │  • "Why this trade" reasoning                             │    ║
║   │  [✅ Execute] [❌ Dismiss] [🔕 Snooze]                    │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │         ▼                                                │    ║
║   │  3. ORDER PLACED                                          │    ║
║   │  ─────────────                                            │    ║
║   │  Order sent to MT5 via EA / Bridge:                       │    ║
║   │  • Type: MARKET / LIMIT / STOP                            │    ║
║   │  • Redis Queue → EA → MT5 → Broker                       │    ║
║   │  • Status: PENDING → EXECUTED → ACTIVE                    │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │         ▼                                                │    ║
║   │  4. LIVE MONITORING                                        │    ║
║   │  ────────────────                                          │    ║
║   │  Dashboard updates in real-time:                           │    ║
║   │  • Position P&L (live MT5 sync)                           │    ║
║   │  • TP1 hit → notify + suggest partial close               │    ║
║   │  • SL approaching → risk alert                             │    ║
║   │  • Move to BE → "Risk-free now ✅"                       │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │         ▼                                                │    ║
║   │  5. TRADE CLOSED                                           │    ║
║   │  ─────────────                                             │    ║
║   │  TP or SL hit → MT5 closes position:                       │    ║
║   │  • Auto-capture to Journal                                │    ║
║   │  • Emotion tag prompt                                      │    ║
║   │  • Screenshot auto-attached                                │    ║
║   │  • Signal outcome recorded (WIN/LOSS/BE)                   │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │         ▼                                                │    ║
║   │  6. ANALYTICS UPDATED                                       │    ║
║   │  ──────────────────                                         │    ║
║   │  All metrics recalculated in real-time:                     │    ║
║   │  • Win rate · Profit factor · Sharpe · Drawdown            │    ║
║   │  • Equity curve updated                                     │    ║
║   │  • Goal tracker progress                                    │    ║
║   │  • AI Learning: outcome → improve future signals           │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ⏱️ COMPLETE CYCLE: Signal→Order→Execute→Journal→Analytics      ║
║   💰 NO MANUAL DATA ENTRY. Fully automated.                       ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 📊 Trading Rules Engine

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   EA v4.0 PRO — Auto-Enforced Trading Rules                      ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  🛑 DAILY LOSS LIMIT                                     │    ║
║   │  • Max daily loss: $600 (IDR 600rb equivalent)          │    ║
║   │  • Hit → auto-lock all new entries                       │    ║
║   │  • Reset: Next trading day                                │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  📊 MAX TRADES PER DAY                                   │    ║
║   │  • Limit: 10 trades/day                                   │    ║
║   │  • Hit → alert + suggest review                          │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  ⚠️ CONSECUTIVE LOSS PROTECTION                           │    ║
║   │  • 3 losses in a row → auto-lockout 5 hours              │    ║
║   │  • Psychology alert: "Take a break. Review your trades." │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  📈 SMART BREAKEVEN                                       │    ║
║   │  • Move SL to BE after +300 points (XAUUSD)              │    ║
║   │  • Risk-free trade notification                           │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  📊 PARTIAL CLOSE STRATEGY                                 │    ║
║   │  • TP1 hit → 50% closed, SL → BE                         │    ║
║   │  • TP2 hit → 30% closed                                  │    ║
║   │  • TP3 hit → 20% closed (full exit)                       │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  🔒 NO EA LAYER                                          │    ║
║   │  • Block new entry if position already active            │    ║
║   │  • Prevent duplicate entries on same pair                │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  🌍 KILL ZONE DETECTION                                   │    ║
║   │  • Only trade during London + NY kill zones              │    ║
║   │  • Outside KZ → entry blocked (override-able)            │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```
