## 🔒 MARGIN — Risk Monitoring

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   Margin is your lifeline. Never let it run too low.             ║
║                                                                   ║
║   MARGIN METER:                                                    ║
║   ────────────                                                     ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  MARGIN LEVEL: 1,625%                                    │   ║
║   │  ████████████████████████████████████████░░░░░░░░░░░░░   │   ║
║   │  🟢 SAFE ZONE (>500%)                                    │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  Used Margin:    $315.00    (2 positions)                │   ║
║   │  Free Margin:    $4,805.50  (available for new trades)  │   ║
║   │  Account Equity: $5,120.50                               │   ║
║   │  Leverage:       1:500                                    │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   MARGIN LEVEL ZONES:                                              ║
║   ─────────────────                                                ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │  ZONE          LEVEL         STATUS      ACTION          │   ║
║   │  ────          ─────         ──────      ──────          │   ║
║   │  🟢 SAFE       > 500%        Healthy     Trade freely   │   ║
║   │  🟡 CAUTION    200-500%      Moderate    Reduce size    │   ║
║   │  🟠 WARNING    100-200%      Risky       No new trades  │   ║
║   │  🔴 DANGER     < 100%        MARGIN CALL Close positions │   ║
║   │  🚫 STOP OUT   < 50%         LIQUIDATION System closes  │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   MARGIN CALCULATOR:                                               ║
║   ─────────────────                                                ║
║   • Pre-trade margin check: "This trade uses $150 margin. OK?"   ║
║   • Multi-position margin: $315 used / $4,805 free = 6.2%        ║
║   • Max position calculator: "You can open 15 more 0.03 lots"   ║
║   • Leverage impact: "1:500 = 0.2% margin per position"          ║
║                                                                   ║
║   SMART ALERTS:                                                    ║
║   ────────────                                                     ║
║   • Margin < 300% → ⚠️ "Reduce position sizes now"               ║
║   • Margin < 150% → 🚫 "No new trades. Close some positions."    ║
║   • New trade would push margin < 200% → block entry             ║
║   • Free margin < $500 → 💰 "Consider deposit or reduce lots"   ║
║                                                                   ║
║   SOURCE: MT5 AccountInfo() · margin, margin_free, margin_level  ║
║   ⏱️ Updates: Every position change + every 30s                     ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

║   • Recent trades (time, price, quantity)                         ║
║   • Funding rate (futures, 8h intervals)                          ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ADVANTAGE OVER MT5 CRYPTO:                                       ║
║   ─────────────────────────                                       ║
║   • Real market volume (not broker CFD)                           ║
║   • Order book depth for liquidity analysis                      ║
║   • Funding rates → market sentiment                              ║
║   • More altcoins than MT5                                        ║
║   • 24/7 data (MT5 crypto has gaps)                              ║
║                                                                   ║

# 🧠 BACKEND MAPPING

> **"The Server-Side Blueprint. Every service. Every port. Every worker."**

## 🏗️ Service Architecture

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                    NGINX PROXY :80/:443                   │    ║
║   │                    SSL · Routing · Static                │    ║
║   └────────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                            │                                      ║
║   ┌────────────────────────┴────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                  GAS GATEWAY :8000                        │    ║
║   │            Auth JWT · Rate Limit · Proxy Router          │    ║
║   └───────┬────────────┬────────────┬────────────┬──────────┘    ║
║           │            │            │            │               ║
║   ┌───────┴───┐ ┌─────┴─────┐ ┌───┴──────┐ ┌──┴──────────┐    ║
║   │ CORE API  │ │ AI ENGINE │ │ TRADING  │ │ DATA & INFRA│    ║
║   └───────────┘ └───────────┘ └──────────┘ └─────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║

## 🔴 CORE API LAYER

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║

# 🔧 CORE SERVICES

> **"Every microservice. Every responsibility. Every dependency."**

## 🔴 API & GATEWAY

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────┬──────┬──────────────────────────────────┐ ║
║   │ SERVICE          │ PORT │ DETAILS                           │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────┼──────────────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ gas-gateway-api  │ 8000 │ Main entry. JWT auth. Rate limit.│ ║
║   │                  │      │ Proxy /terminal/* to :8085        │ ║
║   │                  │      │ Proxy /signal/* to :8106          │ ║
║   │                  │      │ All traffic goes through here     │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────┼──────────────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ gas-auth-service │ 8001 │ Supabase JWT validation           │ ║
║   │                  │      │ User registration · Login          │ ║
║   │                  │      │ Role-based access control          │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────┼──────────────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ gas-user-service │ 8002 │ User profiles · Preferences       │ ║
║   │                  │      │ Trading settings · Risk limits     │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────┼──────────────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ gas-billing      │ 8004 │ Credit management · Plans          │ ║
║   │                  │      │ Subscription · Boosters            │ ║
║   │                  │      │ Atomic credit deduction (Lua)      │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────┼──────────────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ gas-terminal-be  │ 8085 │ Main backend API                   │ ║
║   │                  │      │ /analyze · /journal · /backtest   │ ║
║   │                  │      │ /chat · /settings · /subscription │ ║
║   │                  │      │ Orchestrates all microservices    │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────┼──────────────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ gas-web-backend  │ 8005 │ Web-specific API endpoints         │ ║
║   │                  │      │ Dashboard data aggregation         │ ║
║   └──────────────────┴──────┴──────────────────────────────────┘ ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

# 🏗️ RECOMMENDED STACK

> **"The Technology Powering Golden Dragon."**

## 🐍 Backend Stack

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────┐ ║
║   │ LAYER            │ TECHNOLOGY                                │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ Language         │ Python 3.12+                             │ ║
║   │ Framework        │ FastAPI (async) · Uvicorn                │ ║
║   │ API Docs         │ OpenAPI / Swagger (auto-generated)       │ ║
║   │ Validation       │ Pydantic v2                              │ ║
║   │ Auth             │ JWT (Supabase) · python-jose             │ ║
║   │ Async            │ asyncio · httpx · aiohttp                │ ║
║   │ Background       │ Celery / BullMQ (Redis-backed)           │ ║
║   │ WebSocket        │ FastAPI WebSocket · wsproto              │ ║
║   │ Logging          │ Loguru · Structlog (JSON format)         │ ║
║   │ Testing          │ pytest · pytest-asyncio · httpx           │ ║
║   └──────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────┘ ║
║                                                                   ║

║   🎯 SIGNAL INTELLIGENCE   → Signal templates + grading criteria  ║
║   🎓 EDUCATION TOOLS       → Learning materials + AI prompts     ║
║                                                                   ║
║   20 battle-tested, AI-optimized trading strategies.              ║
║   Each strategy is a complete package:                             ║
║                                                                   ║
║   📖 Strategy Doc     — What, When, How, Risk Rules              ║
║   📊 Backtest Data    — Historical performance proof             ║
║   🎯 Signal Template  — Entry/Exit rules for AI generation       ║
║   🤖 AI Prompt        — Custom prompt for strategy-specific AI   ║
║   📈 Pine Script      — TradingView indicator code               ║
║   ⚙️ Risk Profile     — Max DD, RR minimum, session rules       ║
║                                                                   ║
║   STRATEGY CATEGORIES:                                             ║
║   ──────────────────                                               ║
║   ⚡ SCALPING (5)     M1-M5 · ICT · Order Flow · Fast setups     ║
║   📊 INTRADAY (5)     H1-H4 · SMC · Kill Zones · Trend trades    ║
║   📈 SWING (5)        D1-W1 · Macro · Structure · Position       ║

║                                                                   ║

║                                                                   ║

# 🗄️ DATABASE MAPPING

> **"The Data Layer. Every table. Every relationship. Every index."**

## 📊 Core Tables

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────┐ ║
║   │ TABLE            │ PURPOSE                                   │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ users            │ User accounts · Profile · Auth            │ ║
║   │ subscriptions    │ Plan tiers · Credits · Expiry             │ ║
║   │ analyses         │ AI analysis results · History             │ ║
║   │ signals          │ Generated signals · Grades · Outcomes     │ ║
║   │ journals         │ Trade journal entries · Auto-captured     │ ║
║   │ backtests        │ Backtest configs + results                │ ║
║   │ watchlists       │ Custom user watchlists                    │ ║
║   │ alerts           │ User alert configurations                 │ ║
║   │ chat_history     │ AI chat conversations                     │ ║
║   │ market_data      │ OHLC + Tick data (time-series)            │ ║
║   │ positions        │ Active + closed positions from MT5        │ ║
║   │ accounts         │ MT5 account snapshots                     │ ║
║   │ economic_events  │ Calendar events (ForexFactory)            │ ║
║   │ sentiment_data   │ Fear & Greed · News sentiment             │ ║
║   │ credit_logs      │ Credit usage audit trail                  │ ║
║   │ agent_logs       │ AI agent execution logs                   │ ║
║   │ model_usage      │ Per-model token tracking                  │ ║
║   │ notifications    │ Notification delivery log                 │ ║
║   └──────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────┘ ║
║                                                                   ║
║   DATABASE:      PostgreSQL 16 (Supabase)                         ║
║   CACHE:         Redis 7 (response cache + session + queue)       ║
║   OBJECTS:       MinIO (screenshots, PDFs, models)                ║
║   VECTORS:       ChromaDB (RAG embeddings)                        ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 👤 users

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────┬──────────────┬──────────────────────────┐ ║
║   │ COLUMN           │ TYPE         │ DESCRIPTION               │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ id               │ UUID (PK)    │ Unique user ID            │ ║
║   │ email            │ VARCHAR(255) │ User email (unique)       │ ║
║   │ name             │ VARCHAR(100) │ Display name              │ ║
║   │ avatar_url       │ TEXT         │ Profile photo URL         │ ║
║   │ plan             │ VARCHAR(20)  │ free/premium/ultimate     │ ║
║   │ role             │ VARCHAR(20)  │ user/admin                │ ║
║   │ credits          │ INTEGER      │ Available credits          │ ║
║   │ credits_used     │ INTEGER      │ Lifetime credits used      │ ║
║   │ mt5_login        │ INTEGER      │ MT5 account number        │ ║
║   │ mt5_server       │ VARCHAR(50)  │ Broker server name        │ ║
║   │ preferences      │ JSONB        │ User settings JSON          │ ║
║   │ trading_style    │ VARCHAR(20)  │ scalping/intraday/swing    │ ║
║   │ experience_level │ VARCHAR(20)  │ beginner/intermediate/pro  │ ║
║   │ timezone         │ VARCHAR(50)  │ User timezone              │ ║
║   │ language         │ VARCHAR(5)   │ id/en                      │ ║
║   │ is_active        │ BOOLEAN      │ Account active status      │ ║
║   │ last_login       │ TIMESTAMP    │ Last login time            │ ║
║   │ created_at       │ TIMESTAMP    │ Account creation           │ ║
║   │ updated_at       │ TIMESTAMP    │ Last update                │ ║
║   └──────────────────┴──────────────┴──────────────────────────┘ ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 💬 conversations

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────┬──────────────┬──────────────────────────┐ ║
║   │ COLUMN           │ TYPE         │ DESCRIPTION               │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ id               │ UUID (PK)    │ Unique conversation ID    │ ║
║   │ user_id          │ UUID (FK)    │ → users.id                │ ║
║   │ title            │ VARCHAR(200) │ Auto-generated title      │ ║
║   │ mode             │ VARCHAR(20)  │ chat/analyze/signal/etc   │ ║
║   │ model            │ VARCHAR(50)  │ AI model used             │ ║
║   │ messages         │ JSONB        │ Full message history       │ ║
║   │ message_count    │ INTEGER      │ Total messages             │ ║
║   │ tokens_used      │ INTEGER      │ Total tokens consumed      │ ║
║   │ cost_usd         │ DECIMAL(8,4) │ Total AI cost              │ ║
║   │ is_archived      │ BOOLEAN      │ Archived by user           │ ║
║   │ is_pinned        │ BOOLEAN      │ Pinned to top              │ ║
║   │ tags             │ TEXT[]       │ User tags for search       │ ║
║   │ created_at       │ TIMESTAMP    │ First message time         │ ║
║   │ updated_at       │ TIMESTAMP    │ Last message time          │ ║
║   └──────────────────┴──────────────┴──────────────────────────┘ ║
║                                                                   ║
║   INDEXES: user_id · created_at DESC · mode · is_pinned           ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🎯 signals

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────┬──────────────┬──────────────────────────┐ ║
║   │ COLUMN           │ TYPE         │ DESCRIPTION               │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ id               │ UUID (PK)    │ Unique signal ID          │ ║
║   │ user_id          │ UUID (FK)    │ → users.id                │ ║
║   │ pair             │ VARCHAR(20)  │ XAUUSD, EURUSD...         │ ║
║   │ direction        │ VARCHAR(5)   │ BUY / SELL                │ ║
║   │ entry_low        │ DECIMAL(12,5)│ Entry zone low            │ ║
║   │ entry_high       │ DECIMAL(12,5)│ Entry zone high           │ ║
║   │ stop_loss        │ DECIMAL(12,5)│ SL price                  │ ║
║   │ take_profit_1    │ DECIMAL(12,5)│ TP1 price                 │ ║
║   │ take_profit_2    │ DECIMAL(12,5)│ TP2 price                 │ ║
║   │ take_profit_3    │ DECIMAL(12,5)│ TP3 price                 │ ║
║   │ lot_size         │ DECIMAL(10,4)│ Suggested lot size        │ ║
║   │ risk_reward      │ DECIMAL(5,2) │ RR ratio (TP1)            │ ║
║   │ grade            │ VARCHAR(5)   │ A+ / A / B / C / REJECT   │ ║
║   │ confidence       │ INTEGER      │ 0-100 confidence %         │ ║
║   │ risk_score       │ INTEGER      │ 0-100 risk assessment      │ ║
║   │ trading_style    │ VARCHAR(20)  │ scalping/intraday/swing    │ ║
║   │ timeframe        │ VARCHAR(5)   │ H4, H1, M15...            │ ║
║   │ session          │ VARCHAR(20)  │ Asian/London/NY            │ ║
║   │ source           │ VARCHAR(20)  │ AI / Pine / Hybrid / Manual│ ║
║   │ analysis_id      │ UUID (FK)    │ → analyses.id              │ ║
║   │ status           │ VARCHAR(20)  │ ACTIVE/EXPIRED/EXECUTED    │ ║
║   │ outcome          │ VARCHAR(10)  │ WIN / LOSS / BE / PENDING  │ ║
║   │ outcome_pips     │ DECIMAL(8,2) │ Actual pips result         │ ║
║   │ outcome_profit   │ DECIMAL(10,2)│ Actual USD profit          │ ║
║   │ model_used       │ VARCHAR(50)  │ AI model that generated    │ ║
║   │ tokens_used      │ INTEGER      │ Tokens consumed             │ ║
║   │ is_executed      │ BOOLEAN      │ Trader took this signal    │ ║
║   │ is_notified      │ BOOLEAN      │ Notification sent          │ ║
║   │ expires_at       │ TIMESTAMP    │ Signal validity expiry     │ ║
║   │ created_at       │ TIMESTAMP    │ Signal generated time      │ ║
║   │ updated_at       │ TIMESTAMP    │ Last update                │ ║
║   └──────────────────┴──────────────┴──────────────────────────┘ ║
║                                                                   ║
║   INDEXES: user_id · pair · grade · created_at DESC · outcome     ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 📓 journals

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────┬──────────────┬──────────────────────────┐ ║
║   │ COLUMN           │ TYPE         │ DESCRIPTION               │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ id               │ UUID (PK)    │ Unique journal ID         │ ║
║   │ user_id          │ UUID (FK)    │ → users.id                │ ║
║   │ signal_id        │ UUID (FK)    │ → signals.id (nullable)   │ ║
║   │ analysis_id      │ UUID (FK)    │ → analyses.id (nullable)  │ ║
║   │ pair             │ VARCHAR(20)  │ XAUUSD, EURUSD...         │ ║
║   │ direction        │ VARCHAR(5)   │ BUY / SELL                │ ║
║   │ entry_price      │ DECIMAL(12,5)│ Entry price               │ ║
║   │ exit_price       │ DECIMAL(12,5)│ Exit price                │ ║
║   │ lot_size         │ DECIMAL(10,4)│ Position size             │ ║
║   │ profit_usd       │ DECIMAL(10,2)│ Net P&L in USD            │ ║
║   │ trade_result     │ VARCHAR(10)  │ WIN / LOSS / BE            │ ║
║   │ profit_pips      │ DECIMAL(8,2) │ Net P&L in pips           │ ║
║   │ duration_min     │ INTEGER      │ Trade duration (minutes)   │ ║
║   │ setup_tag        │ VARCHAR(30)  │ SMC/ICT/Breakout/SR        │ ║
║   │ emotion_tag      │ VARCHAR(20)  │ Calm/FOMO/Revenge/Confident│ ║
║   │ mistake_tag      │ VARCHAR(30)  │ No SL/Oversize/Early Exit  │ ║
║   │ session          │ VARCHAR(20)  │ Asian/London/NY            │ ║
║   │ trading_style    │ VARCHAR(20)  │ scalping/intraday/swing    │ ║
║   │ timeframe        │ VARCHAR(5)   │ H4, H1, M15...            │ ║
║   │ entry_screenshot │ TEXT         │ MinIO URL entry chart      │ ║
║   │ exit_screenshot  │ TEXT         │ MinIO URL exit chart       │ ║
║   │ notes            │ TEXT         │ Trader notes               │ ║
║   │ ai_insights      │ JSONB        │ AI-generated insights      │ ║
║   │ is_manual        │ BOOLEAN      │ Manual vs auto-captured    │ ║
║   │ created_at       │ TIMESTAMP    │ Trade close time           │ ║
║   └──────────────────┴──────────────┴──────────────────────────┘ ║
║                                                                   ║
║   INDEXES: user_id · pair · created_at DESC · setup_tag · emotion │ ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 📊 market_snapshots

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────┬──────────────┬──────────────────────────┐ ║
║   │ COLUMN           │ TYPE         │ DESCRIPTION               │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ id               │ UUID (PK)    │ Unique snapshot ID        │ ║
║   │ symbol           │ VARCHAR(20)  │ XAUUSD, EURUSD...         │ ║
║   │ timeframe        │ VARCHAR(5)   │ H4, H1, M15...            │ ║
║   │ price_bid        │ DECIMAL(12,5)│ Bid price at snapshot     │ ║
║   │ price_ask        │ DECIMAL(12,5)│ Ask price at snapshot     │ ║
║   │ spread           │ DECIMAL(8,2) │ Spread in pips            │ ║
║   │ bias             │ VARCHAR(10)  │ BULLISH/BEARISH/NEUTRAL   │ ║
║   │ bias_confidence  │ INTEGER      │ 0-100 confidence %         │ ║
║   │ structure_state  │ JSONB        │ Structure per TF           │ ║
║   │ indicators       │ JSONB        │ 50+ indicator readings     │ ║
║   │ patterns         │ JSONB        │ Detected patterns          │ ║
║   │ regime           │ VARCHAR(20)  │ Trending/Ranging/Volatile  │ ║
║   │ session          │ VARCHAR(20)  │ Asian/London/NY            │ ║
║   │ liquidity_zones  │ JSONB        │ EQH/EQL/OB/FVG zones       │ ║
║   │ volatility       │ JSONB        │ ATR/BB/VIX metrics         │ ║
║   │ macro_context    │ JSONB        │ Calendar + fundamental     │ ║
║   │ snapshot_at      │ TIMESTAMP    │ When snapshot was taken    │ ║
║   │ created_at       │ TIMESTAMP    │ Record creation            │ ║
║   └──────────────────┴──────────────┴──────────────────────────┘ ║
║                                                                   ║
║   INDEXES: symbol · timeframe · snapshot_at DESC                  ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🔄 CI/CD Pipeline

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  GitHub Repo → GitHub Actions → Docker Build → Deploy    │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  1. PUSH to main branch                                   │    ║
║   │  2. GitHub Actions triggers:                               │    ║
║   │     • Run tests (pytest · eslint)                         │    ║
║   │     • Build Docker images                                  │    ║
║   │     • Push to container registry                           │    ║
║   │     • SSH to VPS → docker compose pull                     │    ║
║   │     • docker compose up -d (rolling update)               │    ║
║   │  3. Health check → verify all services                     │    ║
║   │  4. Rollback on failure (auto)                             │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  DEPLOY TRIGGERS:                                          │    ║
║   │  • Push to main → production deploy                        │    ║
║   │  • Push to staging → staging deploy                        │    ║
║   │  • Manual trigger → force deploy                           │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 💰 Infrastructure Cost

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────┐ ║
║   │ RESOURCE         │ MONTHLY COST                              │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ VPS (4vCPU/16GB) │ ~$30/mo (Hetzner CX42)                  │ ║
║   │ Supabase         │ $0 (free tier) / $25 (pro)               │ ║
║   │ Cloudflare Pages │ $0 (free tier)                            │ ║
║   │ Cloudflare DNS   │ $0 (free tier)                            │ ║
║   │ Email (Resend)   │ $0 (free 100/day) / $20 (pro)            │ ║
║   │ Domain           │ ~$12/year (gasstrategyai.xyz)            │ ║
║   ├──────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤ ║
║   │ TOTAL INFRA      │ ~$30-50/month                            │ ║
║   │ AI COSTS         │ Variable (~$0.50/user/day)               │ ║
║   └──────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────┘ ║
║                                                                   ║
║   SCALING:                                                         ║
║   ───────                                                         ║
║   < 100 users:     Single VPS 4vCPU/16GB ($30/mo)                ║
║   100-1K users:    + Load Balancer + 2nd VPS ($250/mo)           ║
║   1K-10K users:    Kubernetes cluster ($500-1000/mo)             ║
║   10K-50K users:   Multi-region K8s + CDN ($2000+/mo)           ║
║   50K+ users:      Enterprise K8s + Dedicated DB ($5000+/mo)    ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🖥️ VPS / CLOUD SPECS

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   PRIMARY VPS — Hetzner / DigitalOcean / Vultr                   ║
║   ─────────────────────────────────────────                       ║
║   OS:       Ubuntu 22.04 LTS                                     ║
║   CPU:      4 vCPU (AMD EPYC / Intel Xeon)                       ║
║   RAM:      16 GB DDR4                                            ║
║   DISK:     160 GB NVMe SSD                                      ║
║   NET:      1 Gbps · Unlimited transfer                           ║
║   IP:       Static IPv4 + IPv6                                    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   WHAT RUNS ON VPS:                                                ║
║   ────────────────                                                 ║
║   • Docker Engine + 25 containers                                 ║
║   • Nginx reverse proxy (SSL via Certbot)                        ║
║   • All GAS microservices (API + AI + Trading + Data)            ║
║   • Redis (cache + queue + pub/sub)                               ║
║   • MinIO (object storage)                                        ║
║   • ChromaDB (vector database)                                    ║
║   • Prometheus + Grafana + Loki (monitoring)                     ║
║   • MT5 Docker VNC (trading terminal)                             ║
║                                                                   ║
║   WHAT'S EXTERNAL:                                                 ║
║   ───────────────                                                  ║
║   ☁️ Supabase        — PostgreSQL (managed, free tier)            ║
║   ☁️ Cloudflare      — Frontend hosting + DNS + CDN               ║
║   ☁️ AI APIs         — Anthropic · OpenAI · Google · OpenRouter  ║
║   📧 Resend          — Email delivery                              ║
║                                                                   ║
║   BACKUP STRATEGY:                                                 ║
║   ───────────────                                                  ║
║   • PostgreSQL → Supabase auto-backup (daily)                    ║
║   • Redis → AOF + RDB (disk persistence)                          ║
║   • MinIO → Sync to external S3 (weekly)                          ║
║   • Docker configs → Git repository                                ║
║   • .env secrets → 1Password / Vault                              ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🏭 SERIOUS PRODUCTION

> **"Scaled. Redundant. Enterprise-Grade."**

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  🖥️ VPS 1 — APP SERVER           🖥️ VPS 2 — DATA SERVER │    ║
║   │  16vCPU · 64GB · NVMe 400GB     16vCPU · 64GB · NVMe 800GB│   ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  • Gateway · Terminal · AI       • PostgreSQL (primary)   │    ║
║   │  • AI Orchestrator · Signal      • Redis (cache + queue) │    ║
║   │  • Risk · Journal · Strategy     • MinIO (objects)        │    ║
║   │  • Nginx (SSL)                   • ChromaDB (vectors)    │    ║
║   │  • MT5 Docker VNC                • Prometheus · Grafana  │    ║
║   │                                 • Loki (logs)           │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  🖥️ VPS 3 — WORKER SERVER         ☁️ EXTERNAL            │    ║
║   │  8vCPU · 32GB · NVMe 200GB                                │    ║
║   │                                 • Cloudflare CDN + DNS  │    ║
║   │  • Celery Workers (AI tasks)    • Supabase (managed DB)  │    ║
║   │  • Backtest Engine              • AWS S3 (backup)       │    ║
║   │  • Screener                     • SendGrid (email)      │    ║
║   │  • TG Bot · Notification        • Anthropic · OpenAI     │    ║
║   │                                 • OpenRouter · Google   │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   HIGH AVAILABILITY:                                              ║
║   ────────────────                                                ║
║   • Load Balancer: Nginx / HAProxy / Cloudflare LB               ║
║   • PostgreSQL 16: Primary-Replica (auto-failover)               ║
║   • Redis 7: Sentinel for auto-failover · 512MB                  ║
║   • Docker: Swarm / Kubernetes                                    ║
║   • Redis: Sentinel (auto-failover) · 512MB cache                ║
║   • Health checks: Every 15s → auto-restart                      ║
║   • Auto-scaling: CPU > 70% → spawn worker                        ║
║                                                                   ║
║   SECURITY:                                                        ║
║   ────────                                                         ║
║   • Firewall: UFW + Cloudflare WAF                                ║
║   • DDoS Protection: Cloudflare                                    ║
║   • Rate Limiting: Gateway + Cloudflare                           ║
║   • SSL: Certbot auto-renew                                       ║
║   • Secrets: HashiCorp Vault / 1Password                          ║
║   • Audit: All AI calls logged + anomaly detection               ║
║                                                                   ║
║   COST:                                                            ║
║   ────                                                             ║
║   VPS 1 (App):         ~$180/mo (16vCPU/64GB)                    ║
║   VPS 2 (Data):        ~$180/mo (16vCPU/64GB)                    ║
║   VPS 3 (Worker):      ~$80/mo (8vCPU/32GB)                      ║
║   Supabase Pro:         $25/mo                                    ║
║   Cloudflare Pro:       $20/mo                                    ║
║   Email (SendGrid):     $20/mo                                    ║
║   Backup (S3):          ~$10/mo                                   ║
║   ─────────────────────────────────────────                       ║
║   TOTAL INFRA:          ~$540/mo fixed + AI variable              ║
║                                                                   ║
║   CAPACITY: 5,000-50,000 active users                             ║
║   UPTIME: 99.9% (SLA-grade)                                       ║

---

# 🔥 DEPLOYMENT FLOW

> **"From Code to Production. The Complete Deploy Pipeline."**

## 🔄 Deploy Pipeline

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  1. GITHUB PUSH                                          │    ║
║   │  git push origin main → triggers deploy                  │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │         ▼                                                │    ║
║   │  2. GITHUB ACTIONS CI/CD                                  │    ║
║   │  GitHub Actions workflow triggered on push:              │    ║
║   │  • Checkout code                                         │    ║
║   │  • Install dependencies                                  │    ║
║   │  • Run tests (pytest · eslint)                           │    ║
║   │  • Type check (TypeScript)                                │    ║
║   │  • Lint (ruff · black)                                    │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │         ▼                                                │    ║
║   │  3. BUILD                                                 │    ║
║   │  docker build -t gas-{service}:{sha} .                   │    ║
║   │  • Multi-stage build (slim images)                       │    ║
║   │  • Cache layers for speed                                 │    ║
║   │  • Security scan (Trivy/Snyk)                             │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │         ▼                                                │    ║
║   │  4. DOCKER HUB / REGISTRY                                  │    ║
║   │  docker push ghcr.io/gas/{service}:{sha}                 │    ║
║   │  docker tag ghcr.io/gas/{service}:latest                  │    ║
║   │  • ghcr.io (GitHub Container Registry)                    │    ║
║   │  • Docker Hub (public images)                              │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │         ▼                                                │    ║
║   │  5. VPS DEPLOYMENT                                        │    ║
║   │  SSH → VPS (Ubuntu 22.04) · Docker Compose:              │    ║
║   │  • docker compose pull                                    │    ║
║   │  • docker compose up -d (rolling update)                  │    ║
║   │  • Prune old images                                       │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │         ▼                                                │    ║
║   │  6. HEALTH CHECK                                          │    ║
║   │  curl localhost:{port}/health → {"status":"ok"}          │    ║
║   │  • Check all services respond                              │    ║
║   │  • Check DB migrations applied                             │    ║
║   │  • Check Redis connection                                  │    ║
║   │         │                                                │    ║
║   │         ▼                                                │    ║
║   │  7. MONITORING + ALERTS                                    │    ║
║   │  Grafana dashboard · Prometheus metrics · Loki logs      │    ║
║   │  Alerts → Telegram #alerts if anomaly detected            │    ║
║   │  ⏱️ Auto-check every 30s                                    │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  8. SERVICES STARTUP                                       │    ║
║   │  Ordered startup sequence:                                │    ║
║   │  ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │    ║
║   │  │ 1. PostgreSQL · Redis · MinIO · ChromaDB           │  │    ║
║   │  │ 2. MT5 Docker VNC (Exness broker)                   │  │    ║
║   │  │ 3. MT5 Bridge (WS :8110 + REST :8100)              │  │    ║
║   │  │ 4. Core Services (Gateway · Auth · Billing)         │  │    ║
║   │  │ 5. AI Engine (Orchestrator :9003)                    │  │    ║
║   │  │ 6. Trading Services (Signal · Risk · Journal)       │  │    ║
║   │  │ 7. Data Services (Realtime · Calendar · News)      │  │    ║
║   │  │ 8. Nginx (SSL proxy)                                 │  │    ║
║   │  │ 9. Health check ALL services → ✅ System LIVE         │  │    ║
║   │  │ 10. Frontend deploy → Cloudflare Pages (auto)         │  │    ║
║   │  │ 11. DNS propagation → gasstrategyai.xyz LIVE          │  │    ║
║   │  └────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  9. VERIFY + ROLLBACK                                     │    ║
║   │  ✅ All healthy → Deploy complete ✅                     │    ║
║   │  ❌ Any fail → auto-rollback to previous image            │    ║
║   │  📧 Deploy notification → Telegram #deploy                │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ⏱️ TOTAL DEPLOY TIME: 10-20 minutes                            ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🚀 Deploy Commands

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  # FIRST TIME SETUP (GitHub):                           │    ║
║   │  git clone git@github.com:mrj-golden-dragon/gas.git     │    ║
║   │  cd gas && cp .env.example .env                         │    ║
║   │  nano .env  # add API keys + secrets                     │    ║
║   │  docker network create gas-network                        │    ║
║   │  docker compose up -d                                    │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  # DAILY DEPLOY (GitHub → VPS):                         │    ║
║   │  git pull origin main && docker compose pull              │    ║
║   │  && docker compose up -d --remove-orphans                │    ║
║   │  && docker system prune -f                                │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  # HEALTH CHECK:                                         │    ║
║   │  curl localhost:8000/health                              │    ║
║   │  docker compose ps                                       │    ║
║   │  docker compose logs --tail=50 gas-terminal-be           │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   │  # ROLLBACK:                                             │    ║
║   │  docker compose down                                     │    ║
║   │  docker compose -f docker-compose.prev.yml up -d         │    ║
║   │                                                         │    ║
║   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🔌 Unified API Interface

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   ALL providers → ONE standard interface                          ║
║                                                                   ║
║   gas/ai/router.py:                                                ║
║   ────────────────                                                 ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  async def call_model(                                   │   ║
║   │      model: str,           # "claude-sonnet-4-6"         │   ║
║   │      messages: list,       # OpenAI-compatible format    │   ║
║   │      max_tokens: int,                                    │   ║
║   │      temperature: float,                                  │   ║
║   │      stream: bool,                                        │   ║
║   │  ) → ModelResponse:                                      │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  PROVIDER RESOLVER:                                      │   ║
║   │  ┌────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────┐  │   ║
║   │  │ MODEL PREFIX    │ PROVIDER                          │  │   ║
║   │  ├────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤  │   ║
║   │  │ claude-*        │ Anthropic Direct API              │  │   ║
║   │  │ gpt-* o3-*      │ OpenAI Direct API                 │  │   ║
║   │  │ gemini-*        │ Google Vertex AI                  │  │   ║
║   │  │ deepseek/*      │ OpenRouter → DeepSeek              │  │   ║
║   │  │ google/*        │ OpenRouter → Gemini                │  │   ║
║   │  │ x-ai/*          │ OpenRouter → Grok                  │  │   ║
║   │  │ */* (others)    │ OpenRouter → Various               │  │   ║
║   │  │ llama-* mistral*│ Ollama Local                       │  │   ║
║   │  └────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────┘  │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🎯 Smart Routing Logic

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   TASK → MODEL MAPPING                                            ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────────┬──────────────────┬──────────────────┐ ║
║   │ TASK                 │ PRIMARY          │ FALLBACK          │ ║
║   ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────────┤ ║
║   │ Complex Analysis     │ Claude Sonnet 4.6│ GPT-4o           │ ║
║   │ Vision/Chart Read    │ Claude Sonnet 4.6│ GPT-4o Vision    │ ║
║   │ Deep Reasoning       │ DeepSeek R1      │ Claude Sonnet    │ ║
║   │ Fast/Quick Tasks     │ GPT-4o-mini      │ Claude Haiku     │ ║
║   │ Strategy/Backtest    │ Gemini 2.5 Pro   │ Claude Sonnet    │ ║
║   │ Psychology/Mentor    │ Claude Sonnet 4.6│ GPT-4o           │ ║
║   │ Journal Tagging      │ Claude Haiku 4.5 │ GPT-4o-mini      │ ║
║   │ Code Gen (PS/MQL)    │ GPT-4o-mini      │ Claude Haiku     │ ║
║   │ Intent/Routing       │ GPT-4o-mini      │ (local logic)    │ ║
║   │ Embedding/RAG        │ text-embed-3     │ (OpenAI only)    │ ║
║   │ Pure Computation     │ NO AI            │ (free forever)   │ ║
║   └──────────────────────┴──────────────────┴──────────────────┘ ║
║                                                                   ║
║   MODEL SELECTION FACTORS:                                         ║
║   ───────────────────────                                          ║
║   • Task complexity (1-10 scale)                                   ║
║   • User plan tier (limits model access)                           ║
║   • Latency budget (streaming? < 2s? < 60s?)                     ║
║   • Cost budget (per user credit tier)                            ║
║   • Availability (circuit breaker status)                          ║
║   • Recent performance (error rate per model)                      ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🔄 Circuit Breaker + Fallback

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   SELF-HEALING MODEL ROUTING                                     ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  PRIMARY: Claude Sonnet 4.6                              │   ║
║   │      │                                                    │   ║
║   │      ├── ✅ Success → return result                      │   ║
║   │      │                                                    │   ║
║   │      ├── ❌ Fail (1-4) → retry same model                │   ║
║   │      │                                                    │   ║
║   │      ├── ❌ Fail (5) → CIRCUIT BREAKER OPEN              │   ║
║   │      │    │                                                │   ║
║   │      │    ├──► FALLBACK: GPT-4o                           │   ║
║   │      │    │                                                │   ║
║   │      │    └──► Sonnet marked DOWN for 300s                │   ║
║   │      │         Auto-retry after timeout                    │   ║
║   │      │         If still failing → alert admin              │   ║
║   │      │                                                    │   ║
║   │      └── ✅ Fallback succeeds → log incident              │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   │  RESPONSE CACHE:                                          │   ║
║   │  Same pair+TF+style within 60s → skip AI → Redis         │   ║
║   │  Cache hit rate: 40-60% (reduces cost 50-70%)            │   ║
║   │                                                          │   ║
║   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 💰 Cost Optimization

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   WITHOUT Smart Routing:         WITH Smart Routing:              ║
║   ─────────────────────         ───────────────────                ║
║   All tasks → Sonnet            Quick task → GPT-4o-mini          ║
║   $0.09 × 100 calls = $9.00     $0.001 × 40 calls = $0.04        ║
║                                  Standard → Haiku                  ║
║                                  $0.004 × 30 calls = $0.12        ║
║                                  Deep → Sonnet                     ║
║                                  $0.09 × 20 calls = $1.80         ║
║                                  Vision → Sonnet                   ║
║                                  $0.015 × 10 calls = $0.15        ║
║                                  ────────────────────────────     ║
║                                  TOTAL: $2.11                      ║
║                                  SAVINGS: 77%                      ║
║                                                                   ║
║   WITH CACHING (60s TTL):                                         ║
║   40-60% requests skip AI entirely → adds 50-70% savings          ║
║   Effective cost per user/day: ~$0.50 - $1.00                     ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 1.2 💬 CHAT WORKSPACE — AI Analysis On Demand

### Chat Modes

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   MODE              TRIGGER          WHAT IT DOES                 ║
║   ────              ───────          ────────────                 ║
║   Quick Chat        Default          Fast Q&A, explain, teach    ║
║   Full Analysis     /analyze         Full AI pipeline analysis   ║
║   Vision Analysis   Upload chart     Screenshot → AI vision     ║
║   Signal Request    /signal          Generate structured signal  ║
║   Journal Entry     /journal         Log a trade via chat        ║
║   Backtest          /backtest        Run strategy test            ║
║   Screener          /scan            Multi-pair scan              ║
║   Psychology        /psych           Mindset check-in            ║
║   Mentor            /mentor          1-on-1 coaching session     ║
║   Code Gen          /code            Generate Pine Script/MQL    ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

### Full Analysis Pipeline (When User Types "/analyze XAUUSD H4 intraday")

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   STEP 1: CONTEXT GATHERING                                       ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  • Parse: pair=XAUUSD, TF=H4, style=intraday              │  ║
║   │  • Detect: current session (London/NY/Asian)              │  ║
║   │  • Load: user's trading history + psychology profile      │  ║
║   │  • Check: upcoming high-impact news ±30m                  │  ║
║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                            │                                      ║
║                            ▼                                      ║
║   STEP 2: VISION CAPTURE                                          ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  Vision Engine :9504                                       │  ║
║   │  • Playwright opens TradingView chart                      │  ║
║   │  • Screenshots: M5, M15, H1, H4 (scalping → M1,M5,M15,H1)│  ║
║   │  • Compress JPEG q85, max 1024px → base64 encode           │  ║
║   │  ⏱️ ~20-30s                                                │  ║
║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                            │                                      ║
║                            ▼                                      ║
║   STEP 3: TECHNICAL ANALYSIS                                      ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  Parallel calls:                                           │  ║
║   │  • SMC Engine :8006    → OB, FVG, Liquidity, Breaker      │  ║
║   │  • Indicator :8203     → ADX, RSI, MACD, Bollinger, EMA   │  ║
║   │  • Pattern :9501       → H&S, Double Top, Wedge, Flag     │  ║
║   │  • Regime :9503        → Trending/Ranging/Volatile        │  ║
║   │  • MT5 Data :8100      → Live price + OHLC                │  ║
║   │  • Orderflow :8204     → Delta, CVD, Footprint            │  ║
║   │  • Trend :8201         → EMA Cloud, Swing Structure       │  ║
║   │  ⏱️ ~5-10s (parallel)                                   │  ║
║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                            │                                      ║
║                            ▼                                      ║
║   STEP 4: MACRO CONTEXT                                           ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  Parallel calls:                                           │  ║
║   │  • Calendar :9601     → Upcoming events ±2h               │  ║
║   │  • Fundamental :9603  → CPI, GDP, NFP, COT, Interest      │  ║
║   │  • Sentiment :8009    → Fear & Greed, News Tone           │  ║
║   │  • Correlation :8101  → DXY, VIX, Bonds correlation       │  ║
║   │  ⏱️ ~2-5s (parallel)                                    │  ║
║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                            │                                      ║
║                            ▼                                      ║
║   STEP 5: AI SYNTHESIS (Claude Sonnet 4.6)                        ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  Input:                                                    │  ║
║   │  • 4 chart screenshots (base64)                            │  ║
║   │  • Technical data (SMC, Indicators, Pattern, Regime)       │  ║
║   │  • Macro context (Calendar, Fundamental, Sentiment)        │  ║
║   │  • Style-specific prompt (intraday.txt)                    │  ║
║   │                                                            │  ║
║   │  Output: Structured JSON                                   │  ║
║   │  {                                                         │  ║
║   │    observation:   {price_action, structure, key_levels},   │  ║
║   │    reasoning:     {bias, confluences, logic},              │  ║
║   │    trading_plan:  {entry, sl, tp1, tp2, tp3, rr},         │  ║
║   │    risk:          {lot_size, max_drawdown, notes},         │  ║
║   │    journal:       {expected_outcome, setup_quality}        │  ║
║   │  }                                                         │  ║
║   │  ⏱️ ~40-60s                                             │  ║
║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                            │                                      ║
║                            ▼                                      ║
║   STEP 6: RISK VALIDATION                                         ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  Risk Engine :8105                                         │  ║
║   │  • Validate RR ratio ≥ style minimum                      │  ║
║   │  • Calculate lot size (balance × risk%)                    │  ║
║   │  • Check daily drawdown limit                              │  ║
║   │  • Apply Prop Firm rules (if enabled)                      │  ║
║   │  • Flag: GO / CAUTION / NO_TRADE                           │  ║
║   │  ⏱️ ~1-2s                                                │  ║
║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                            │                                      ║
║                            ▼                                      ║
║   STEP 7: FORMAT + RENDER + STREAM                                ║
║   ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  ║
║   │  • Format JSON → Markdown/HTML (per channel)              │  ║
║   │  • Paginate into 4096-char chunks (TG)                    │  ║
║   │  • SSE stream to client                                    │  ║
║   │  • Save to PostgreSQL (analyses table)                     │  ║
║   │  • Cache to Redis (TTL 60s)                                │  ║
║   │  • Deduct credits                                          │  ║
║   │  ⏱️ ~1s                                                 │  ║
║   └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ⏱️ TOTAL TARGET: 70-90 seconds (Vision + AI dominate)          ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🏦 GAS vs BROKER (Penting: Kami Bukan Broker!)

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║   BROKER                          GAS (Golden AI Strategy)        ║
║   ──────                          ────────────────────────        ║
║                                                                   ║
║   Tempat lo buka akun trading     Platform intelligence di atas   ║
║                                   broker lo                       ║
║                                                                   ║
║   Menyediakan:                    Menyediakan:                    ║
║   • Platform MT4/MT5              • AI Analysis & Reasoning       ║
║   • Eksekusi order                • Sinyal dengan struktur        ║
║   • Leverage & spread             • Risk calculator               ║
║   • Deposit & withdrawal          • Auto trade journal            ║
║                                   • Psychology coach              ║
║                                   • Backtest & screener           ║
║                                   • AI Mentor 24/7                ║
║                                                                   ║
║   Broker = TEMPAT eksekusi        GAS = OTAK buat eksekusi       ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   CARA KERJA:                                                     ║
║                                                                   ║
║   ① Lo punya akun di broker (Exness, IC Markets, Binance, etc)  ║
║   ② GAS analisa market → kasih setup + risk plan                ║
║   ③ Lo review → lo yang eksekusi di broker lo sendiri           ║
║   ④ GAS tracking hasil → journal otomatis → improvement plan    ║
║                                                                   ║
║   GAS gak pernah megang duit lo. Gak pernah eksekusi sendiri.    ║
║   Kami platform ANALYTICS. Lo tetap FULL CONTROL.                ║
║                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 🏆 UNIQUE VALUE PROPOSITION

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                   ║
║  1. STYLE-BASED AI ENGINE (Bukan Generic ChatGPT)                ║
║  ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║  │  System ini ngerti beda cara lo trading.                  │   ║
║  │                                                           │   ║
║  │  Scalping ≠ Intraday ≠ Swing ≠ Hold                       │   ║
║  │                                                           │   ║
║  │  Tiap style punya:                                        │   ║
║  │  • Timeframe matrix sendiri (TF1→TF2→TF3→TF4)            │   ║
║  │  • Prompt AI sendiri (scalping.txt, intraday.txt...)     │   ║
║  │  • RR threshold sendiri (1:1.5 / 1:2 / 1:3 / 1:5)       │   ║
║  │  • Concept ICT/SMC sendiri (FVG, OB, breaker, etc)       │   ║
║  │                                                           │   ║
║  │  → AI adapt ke LO, bukan lo yang adapt ke AI.            │   ║
║  └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                   ║
║  2. FULL CYCLE (Bukan Cuma "Entry Mana?")                        ║
║  ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║  │                                                           │   ║
║  │  ANALISIS ──► EKSEKUSI ──► JURNAL ──► REFLEKSI ──► GROW │   ║
║  │                                                           │   ║

║  │                                                           │   ║

║  │  AI Mentor detect:                                        │   ║
║  │  • Pattern FOMO (overtrade, cut profit cepet)             │   ║

║  │  • Pattern hesitation (setup valid tapi skip entry)       │   ║
║  │                                                           │   ║
║  │  → Seperti punya trading coach pribadi 24/7.              │   ║

║  │                                                           │   ║

║                                                                   ║

║       Analysis → Execution → Journal → Reflection → Growth.      ║
║       We never stop at "BUY/SELL".                               ║
║                                                                   ║
║  III. PROOF, NOT PROMISE                                         ║
║       Every claim backed by data. Every trade journaled.         ║
║       Every edge verified. No "trust me bro".                    ║
║                                                                   ║
║  IV.  MENTAL GAME FIRST                                          ║
║       Technical analysis is 20%. Psychology is 80%.              ║
║       Our AI checks your mindset before your setup.               ║
║                                                                   ║
║  V.   ACCESSIBLE, NOT CHEAP                                      ║
║       $2.99 entry → $19.99 pro. Quality AI, fair pricing.        ║
║       No ads. No data selling. Trader pays, trader wins.         ║
║                                                                   ║
║  VI.  BROKER-AGNOSTIC                                            ║

## 🔄 AI ANALYSIS PIPELINE (End-to-End Flow)

```
User Request: "Analisa XAUUSD H4 intraday, kasih full setup"

  ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
  ║  STEP 1: GATEWAY VALIDATION                    ~50ms            ║
  ╠══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
  ║  JWT Verify → Check Credits → Rate Limit → Route to Terminal    ║
  ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
                                    │
                                    ▼
  ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
  ║  STEP 2: VISION CAPTURE                       ~20-30s           ║
  ╠══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
  ║  Playwright buka 4 chart TradingView (M5, M15, H1, H4)         ║
  ║  Screenshot → compress JPEG q85 → base64 encode                  ║
  ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
                                    │
                                    ▼
  ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
  ║  STEP 3: FEATURE EXTRACTION                   ~5-10s            ║
  ╠══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
  ║  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐          ║
  ║  │ SMC Engine   │  │ Indicator    │  │ Regime Det   │          ║
  ║  │ OB·FVG·Liq   │  │ ADX·RSI·MACD │  │ Trend/Range   │          ║
  ║  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘          ║
  ║                                                                  ║
  ║  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐          ║
  ║  │ Pattern Det  │  │ MT5 Data     │  │ Fundamental  │          ║
  ║  │ Chart Patterns│  │ Live Prices  │  │ Macro Context │          ║
  ║  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘          ║
  ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
                                    │
                                    ▼
  ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
  ║  STEP 4: AI VISION + REASONING                ~40-60s           ║
  ╠══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
  ║  Claude Sonnet 4.6 receives:                                     ║
  ║    • 4 chart screenshots (base64)                                ║
  ║    • All feature data (SMC + Indicators + Regime + Pattern)      ║
  ║    • Market context (Fundamental + Calendar + Sentiment)         ║
  ║    • Trading style prompt (intraday.txt)                         ║
  ║                                                                   ║
  ║  Output JSON:                                                    ║
  ║    {                                                              ║
  ║      "observation":     {...},   // Price action + structure      ║
  ║      "reasoning":       {...},   // Logic + confluences           ║
  ║      "trading_plan":    {...},   // Entry/SL/TP/RR                ║
  ║      "risk_management": {...},   // Lot size + max drawdown       ║
  ║      "journal_backtest":{...}    // Expected outcome              ║
  ║    }                                                              ║
  ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
                                    │
                                    ▼
  ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
  ║  STEP 5: RISK VALIDATION                      ~2-5s             ║
  ╠══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
  ║  Risk Engine:                                                    ║
  ║    • Validate RR ratio (min threshold per style)                 ║
  ║    • Calculate lot size (account balance + risk %)               ║
  ║    • Check daily drawdown limit                                  ║
  ║    • Mark as "no_trade" if risk criteria not met                 ║
  ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
                                    │
                                    ▼
  ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
  ║  STEP 6: FORMAT + RENDER                      ~1-2s             ║
  ╠══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
  ║  Formatter: JSON → Plain text per section                        ║
  ║  Renderer:  Plain text → MarkdownV2 (TG) / HTML (Web)           ║
  ║  Paginated: Auto-split 4096 chars per chunk                      ║
  ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
                                    │
                                    ▼
  ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
  ║  STEP 7: RESPONSE + SAVE                       ~50ms            ║
  ╠══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
  ║  SSE Stream → User (Web/TG/Mobile)                               ║
  ║  Save to: analyses table (PostgreSQL)                            ║
  ║  Cache: Redis TTL 60s                                            ║
  ║  Deduct: Credits from user account                               ║
  ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

  ⏱️  Total Target: 70-90 detik (Vision + AI dominate)
  🎯  Optimization Target: ≤60 detik
```

## 🤖 AI MODELS + ROUTING

```
╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                    AI MODEL ROUTING                              ║
╠══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                  ║
║  TASK TYPE         →  MODEL              →  PROVIDER            ║
║  ─────────────────     ──────────────        ──────────          ║
║  observation        →  claude-sonnet-4-6  →  Anthropic          ║
║  vision/screenshot  →  claude-sonnet-4-6  →  Anthropic          ║
║  reasoning/deep     →  deepseek-r1        →  OpenRouter         ║
║  quick/fast         →  gpt-4o-mini        →  OpenAI             ║
║  backtest           →  gemini-2.5-pro     →  OpenRouter         ║
║  psychology         →  claude-sonnet-4-6  →  Anthropic          ║
║  journal            →  gemini-3-flash     →  OpenRouter         ║
║  mentor             →  claude-haiku-4-5   →  Anthropic          ║
║  scalping/signal    →  gpt-4o             →  OpenAI             ║
║  scanner 20+ pairs  →  deepseek-v3        →  OpenRouter         ║
║  vector embedding   →  text-embed-3-small →  OpenAI             ║
║                                                                  ║
║  MODEL TIER PER PLAN:                                            ║
║  ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────  ║
║  Essential:  DeepSeek(0.8x)·GPT4o-Mini(1x)·Grok(1.5x)·GemPro(5x)║
║  Plus:       Qwen(0.5x)·GemFlash(1x)·Kimi(1.5x)·GemPro(4x)       ║
║  Premium:    GemLite(0.7x)·Haiku(1x)·GemPro(3x)·Opus(5x)         ║
║  Ultimate:   GLM5(0.8x)·Sonnet(1x)·GPT4o(2x)·Opus(3.5x)          ║
║                                                                  ║
║  CIRCUIT BREAKER: 5 failures → timeout 300s → retry              ║
║  RESPONSE CACHE: Redis TTL 60s (identical requests)             ║
║                                                                  ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

## 📡 INTER-SERVICE COMMUNICATION MAP

```
╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                    SERVICE DEPENDENCIES                          ║
╠══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                  ║
║  LEGEND:  ─── HTTP REST    ═══ WebSocket    ··· Redis Pub/Sub   ║
║                                                                  ║
║  redis ───► ALL SERVICES (cache + queue + session)               ║
║  postgres ──► auth, billing, signal, journal, terminal          ║
║                                                                  ║
║  gateway ──► frontend, mt5-ea, telegram-bot                     ║
║  gateway ──► terminal-api (all /terminal/* routes)              ║
║  gateway ──► billing, auth (user management)                    ║
║                                                                  ║
║  terminal-api ──► agent-engine (AI orchestration)               ║
║  terminal-api ──► vision-engine (screenshot)                    ║
║  terminal-api ──► smc-engine, indicator, pattern, regime       ║
║  terminal-api ──► signal, risk, journal, fundamental           ║
║                                                                  ║
║  agent-engine ──► ALL SERVICES (via Tool Registry)              ║
║  agent-engine ··· event-bus (Redis Streams pub/sub)            ║
║                                                                  ║
║  mt5-websocket ═══ mt5-exness (tick stream)                     ║
║  mt5-websocket ──► realtime-hub (broadcast)                     ║
║  realtime-hub ═══ frontend (live prices + signals)             ║
║  realtime-hub ═══ mobile-app (live data)                        ║
║                                                                  ║
║  signal ──► realtime-hub (signal push)                          ║
║  alert-engine ··· realtime-hub (alert dispatch)                 ║
║  telegram-bot ──► terminal-api (analysis requests)              ║
║                                                                  ║
║  SAFE PARALLEL (no dependency conflict):                         ║
║    ✅ gateway + frontend                                         ║
║    ✅ billing + signal                                           ║
║    ✅ auth + mt5-ws                                              ║
║    ✅ smc + indicator + journal                                  ║
║                                                                  ║
║  NEVER PARALLEL:                                                 ║
║    ❌ redis + anything (shared state)                            ║
║    ❌ billing + agent-engine (credit deduction race condition)   ║
║    ❌ signal + realtime-hub (WS state conflict)                  ║
║                                                                  ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

---

## 🔐 SECURITY ARCHITECTURE

```
╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║              DEFENSE IN DEPTH (4 Layers)                         ║
╠══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                  ║
║  LAYER 1 — GATEWAY AUTH                                         ║
║  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║  │  JWT Validation (Supabase) on EVERY external request     │   ║
║  │  Rate Limit: 60 req/min per user · IP blacklist          │   ║
║  │  CORS: gasstrategyai.xyz only                            │   ║
║  │  Request logging + anomaly detection                     │   ║
║  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                           │                                      ║
║                           ▼                                      ║
║  LAYER 2 — INTERNAL SERVICE AUTH                                ║
║  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║  │  X-Internal-Key header required for service-to-service   │   ║
║  │  X-User-ID propagation (gateway injects)                 │   ║
║  │  Service mesh: only gateway can initiate external calls  │   ║
║  │  Internal network: gas-network bridge (isolated)         │   ║
║  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                           │                                      ║
║                           ▼                                      ║
║  LAYER 3 — BILLING + CREDIT                                     ║
║  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║  │  Credit check BEFORE every AI call                       │   ║
║  │  Atomic deduction (Redis Lua script)                     │   ║
║  │  Plan-based feature gating                               │   ║
║  │  Usage tracking per user per model per day               │   ║
║  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                           │                                      ║
║                           ▼                                      ║
║  LAYER 4 — MONITORING + ALERT                                   ║
║  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   ║
║  │  Prometheus metrics: latency, error rate, credit usage   │   ║
║  │  Loki log aggregation: all services unified              │   ║
║  │  Grafana alerts: anomaly detection → Telegram notify     │   ║
║  │  Audit trail: all AI calls logged with user + result     │   ║
║  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   ║
║                                                                  ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```
